You must not leave your post without permission or delay things. If you are an official for a day, you must be responsible for a day. He especially hopes that everyone will work harder than he did when he was in office, because he personally is tired. Now that Mayor Zang has come to lead everyone, you should cheer up and work hard. Mayor Zang has studied municipal administration and has studied in the United States. In the future, there should be achievements that were previously impossible to achieve to satisfy the people's wishes. At 12:00, everyone took a photo together to commemorate the occasion.

Public Security Bureau: The original director, Zeng Yanyi, did not go to the bureau to work after the Northeast Army arrived in Tianjin. The new director, Zhang Xueming, arrived at the bureau at 10:00 AM. All the section chiefs and the directors of the five district offices lined up outside the bureau to welcome him respectfully. Zhang Xueming, Director of the Tianjin Public Security Bureau

Social Affairs Bureau: The original director, Liu Jinsheng, arrived at the bureau at 9:00 AM. At 10:00 AM, the new director, Zang Qifang, arrived at the bureau and summoned the staff for a lecture. He said that there was no need to deny that Chinese society needs to be reformed. However, the starting point of the reform plan should be the cities first, and then the rural areas. Urban social undertakings are directly related to the welfare of the people of the whole country. Looking at various countries in the East and West, the evolution of urban society has affected the changes in the entire society. It is no longer a matter of one country, one city, or one era. Now, let me mention a few key points in social administration to discuss with you: (1) Steady progress and persistence. Social evolution comes gradually and cannot be achieved overnight. The bureau should be bold in carrying out improvements in social undertakings, but it must not be impatient in its intentions. As the saying goes, "Haste makes waste." Today, Chinese society has many deep-rooted problems. If we want to carry out reforms, we must first investigate the pathological conditions clearly, and then use the power of the people and the government to design carefully and do it slowly. (2) Approaching the people. The government is established for the people, and the administration of the bureau is directly related to the people. The staff has a lot of contact with the people in their work. In the future, we hope that the undertakings we organize will be empathetic and must go deep into the people and seek progress together. Do not regard ourselves as officials and raise our status. We should regard ourselves as citizens and think and act like that. We must break the bad habits of bureaucracy and strive to approach the people. Only then will Chinese society have the hope of improvement. (3) Setting an example. The administration of the bureau is different from other agencies, and it is responsible for guiding society. If someone is already corrupted, how can they improve society? Finally, I hope that everyone will be clean and self-disciplined, set an example, and be a model for society and the people. I hope we can all encourage each other. If it does not meet this purpose, either I will leave, or the staff will leave.

Salt Transport Commissioner's Office: When the reporter arrived at the Changlu Salt Transport Commissioner's Office at 10:00 AM, the newly appointed commissioner, Hong Weiguo, was giving a lecture to the staff, repeatedly urging them to work with peace of mind. Those with stronger abilities will be promoted. He then told the reporter that when he was the superintendent of Shanhaiguan Customs, he met Lu Yunshi because of the issue of establishing a Qinhuangdao sub-customs at Lu Transport. Now he is here to replace Lu. Lu has not arrived due to illness.

, and Zhang Guokui, the chief of the general affairs section, is responsible for the handover, which will take about two days to complete. He is not very clear about the salt affairs situation, but from his observations over the years, the national salt affairs generally have many malpractices. The most serious malpractice is that the merchants who handle the affairs add water and mud to exploit the food households, which is obvious to everyone. It is hateful to talk about. After he takes office, he will first eliminate the accumulated malpractices, and at the same time step up the crackdown on smuggling. Those who abide by the rules will be rewarded, and those who control and manipulate will be severely punished. Next, we should expand sales and facilitate transportation, and we should adapt to the circumstances and handle them accordingly. As for the sale of salt, official transportation and official sales are not good policies. In the future, it may be changed to official supervision and merchant sales. Jin Yulun has now been appointed as the director of the Lu Salt Tianjin Wu Sixty-one County Yin'an Official Salt Management Office to take over.

(October 3rd)

Jinpu Railway Handles Traffic

Jinan Communication: She Xu, the chief of the Traffic Department of the Jinpu Railway Administration, came to Jinan yesterday to handle traffic matters. The reporter visited She at the construction room of the Jinan Station of the Jinpu Railway at 10:00 AM this morning (the 4th) and asked about the traffic on the Jinpu Railway and the revenue of the vehicles. She Xu gave the following statement:

Traffic Issues: Regarding the issue of full traffic on the Jinpu Railway, the central government and the Northeast have reached a compromise. He came north this time to handle traffic matters and will go to Dezhou tomorrow (the 5th). It is not yet certain whether he will go north from Dezhou. The most difficult thing now is the lack of vehicles. The Jinpu Railway had four large locomotives, three small reversing locomotives, thirty passenger cars, and seventy freight cars in Tianjin. He does not know if they are all still there at the moment. According to a telegram from Tianjin on the 1st, the Jin army must send the Jinpu Railway's vehicles to Shanxi in order to transport troops. The Jinpu Railway employees believed that if the vehicles were taken away, there would be no way to get through in the future, and it would be difficult to maintain food, so they repeatedly begged the Jin army not to take the vehicles away, but there was no result. Later, he also met with the Northeast Army officers stationed in Tianjin and asked them to mediate, but the Northeast Army was reluctant to interfere because they had just exchanged defenses with the Jin army in Tianjin and had no orders. Therefore, the railway employees broke with the Jin side and almost came to blows. They dismantled all the engine wheel parts and screws to resist and avoided meeting to avoid being forced to drive. Zhu Luyun, the deputy director of the Jinpu Railway, arrived in Tianjin on the 2nd, but the Jin personnel refused to hand over because they claimed that they had to hand over to the Northeast Army, so Zhu has not yet taken over the bureau. In short, full traffic on the Jinpu Railway will have to wait until the Northeast Army takes over the various agencies before it can be handled.

Vehicle Situation: Before the war broke out, the Jinpu Railway had more than 500 passenger and freight cars each, and more than 70 locomotives. Last summer, Feng Yuxiang's army pulled away 400 passenger and freight cars and 21 locomotives. When Tang Shengzhi rebelled, the vehicles disappeared. Last winter, when Shi Yousan's incident occurred, he also took away 300 vehicles and 20 locomotives, which also disappeared. Therefore, it is difficult to talk about reorganizing the Jinpu Railway now. We must wait until the military affairs are settled before we can start. At present, the vehicles used by the General Headquarters, in addition to the five trains originally on the Longhai Railway, have also borrowed 600 vehicles and 18 locomotives from the Jinpu Railway. Qian Zongze, the transportation commander, telegraphed last month that he would return the vehicles in batches, with the ratio of Longhai and Jinpu being one to two. For example, if Longhai returns one train, Jinpu will return two trains. However, due to busy military transportation, only six trains have been returned recently. The Jinpu Railway currently has four passenger trains and three freight trains, totaling nine trains, including others. There are 200 cars of all sizes, seven passenger car locomotives, and nine freight car locomotives, excluding the six new returned trains.

Revenue Situation: The revenue of the Jinpu Railway in the previous two months was very small, and it was very difficult to pay the salaries of the employees. After the military authorities recently returned six trains, the average daily revenue from transporting accumulated goods along the way was 20,000 yuan, which was enough to pay the employees' salaries, but there was no surplus to purchase materials to repair the tracks, bridges, and vehicles. (4th)

He Yingqin Arrives in Jiangxi from Wuhan

Convenes a Military Conference

Determines the Communist Suppression Plan

Nanchang Communication: He Yingqin, the director of the Wuhan Headquarters and the commander-in-chief of the Communist suppression in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces, believes that the Zhu, Mao, Peng, and Huang bandit gangs have fled to the Xinyu and Qingjiang areas and must be eliminated as soon as possible. Therefore, he came to Jiangxi from Wuhan to inspect everything and give instructions to Commander Lu and Division Commander Zhang. On the 2nd of this month, Lu received a telegram from He, stating that he would come to Jiangxi on the 3rd, but was postponed to 10:00 AM on the 5th. Fang took the Xiangjiang water plane to the province. Before He arrived in the province, the heads of various agencies in the city, the leaders of various groups, and the military officers above the regimental commander level gathered at the riverbank of the Mint outside Zhang on the morning of the 5th to welcome him. Those who arrived included Commander Lu, Division Commanders Zhang and Yue, all members of the provincial party headquarters and the provincial government, the Ninth Route Army Headquarters, the 18th Division Headquarters, all officers of the Garrison Command, and more than 1,000 representatives from various industrial, commercial, and academic groups from the provincial government and below. At 10:30 AM, they saw a plane flying from north to south along the Nanxun Road, circling the city once, and then landing in the river outside Zhang. He then disembarked from the water plane amidst the melodious music and shook hands with Lu, Zhang, and other dignitaries. He then took a car with Lu, Zhang, and others to the provincial government, but the security along the way was extremely tight.

After resting at the provincial government, He convened a military conference at 12:00 to discuss all communist suppression plans. Those present included Lu Dipin, Zhang Huizan, Gong Bingfan, Yue Sen, and Lu Xiaochen, among others. First, Lu and Zhang reported on the recent bandit situation, the deployment of the various armies, and the defense work in the provincial capital, and presented various telegrams, charts, and tables. Then, they discussed the allocation of troops and the strategy of attack and defense one by one. The meeting lasted for two hours before it ended. After the military conference ended, the provincial government immediately held a banquet in the Xiyuan Hall to welcome He. During the banquet, Lu gave a welcome speech, He gave a reply, and Provincial Party Member Liu and others gave speeches. After the banquet, He had a long private conversation with Lu, Zhang, and Gong. Then, at about 3:00 PM, he took a car to the airport outside Zhang and boarded the Xiangjiang to return to Wuhan. Xiamen British Concession Land Ownership Issues

The British Concession Will Be Abolished Immediately British Minister Lampton and Envoy to Minister Wang

(September 19, 1930) Regarding the consultation on the resolution of the land ownership issues within the British Concession in Xiamen, I hereby request Your Excellency to confirm this minister's understanding, that is, the deeds given by the British government to foreign nationals for the land parcels in that place should be exchanged for Chinese perpetual lease deeds, with a registration fee of one yuan per mu. From the date that these Chinese perpetual lease deeds are prepared and handed over to the British Consul in Xiamen for distribution to the foreign nationals in that place, the aforementioned concession will be abolished immediately, and all the notes exchanged in 1852 regarding the lease of that place to the British government will be abolished together. As for the Chinese nationals who hold deeds given by the British government in that place, the Chinese authorities will give them appropriate deeds after they submit the deeds given by the British government. The British deeds submitted will be returned by the Chinese authorities to the British Consul for cancellation in the same way as the deeds given to foreign nationals. It is necessary to ask Your Excellency to investigate and reply. Respectfully, To the Honorable Minister of Foreign Affairs of the Great Republic of China, Wang.

Minister Wang's Reply to the British Minister's Note (September 17, 1930 of the Republic of China) In reply to Your Excellency's note of today, regarding the consultation on the resolution of the land ownership issues within the British Concession in Xiamen, I hereby request Your Excellency to confirm this minister's understanding, that is, the deeds given by the British government to foreign nationals for the land parcels in that place should be exchanged for Chinese perpetual lease deeds, with a registration fee of one yuan per mu. From the date that these Chinese perpetual lease deeds are prepared and handed over to the British Consul in Xiamen for distribution to the foreign nationals in that place, the aforementioned concession will be abolished immediately, and all the notes exchanged in 1852 regarding the lease of that place to the British government will be abolished together. As for the Chinese nationals who hold deeds given by the British government in that place, the Chinese authorities will give them appropriate deeds after they submit the deeds given by the British government. The British deeds submitted will be returned by the Chinese authorities to the British Consul for cancellation in the same way as the deeds given to foreign nationals. I have received and approved this, and I, Minister Wang, acknowledge that your understanding of your minister's understanding of the message you received is correct. I should reply for your reference. Respectfully, To the Honorable British Plenipotentiary Minister to China, Lampton.

Minister Wang's Note to the British Minister Lampton (September 17, 1930 of the Republic of China) Regarding the resolution of the land ownership issues within the British Concession in Xiamen, in the documents exchanged today, I, Minister Wang, hereby declare that before the new Chinese national land tax law is implemented in the Xiamen area, all those who hold Chinese perpetual lease deeds in Xiamen in exchange for British Royal deeds will temporarily pay the annual rent according to the current amount collected. It is necessary to ask Your Excellency to investigate and be aware. Respectfully, To the Honorable British Plenipotentiary Minister to China, Lampton.

British Minister Lampton's Reply to Minister Wang's Note (September 17, 1930) Regarding the note received from Your Excellency today, concerning the resolution of the land ownership issues within the British Concession in Xiamen, in the documents exchanged today, I, Minister Wang, hereby declare that before the new Chinese national land tax law is implemented in the Xiamen area, all those who hold Chinese perpetual lease deeds in Xiamen in exchange for British Royal deeds will temporarily pay the annual rent according to the current amount collected. This minister has read and understood that the British government agrees to this statement. I should reply to Your Excellency for your reference. Respectfully, To the Honorable Minister of Foreign Affairs of the Great Republic of China, Wang.

Second Meeting and Third Session of the National Lawyers Association Executive Committee

The National Lawyers Association held its Second Meeting and Third Session of the Executive Committee yesterday, the 4th, at its headquarters in the capital. More than ten executive committee members attended, including Li Sizhen (Xiamen), Qiu Weizhen (Changsha), Wang Shengwu (Anqing), Tang Baoxu (Tianjin), Liu Zuwang and Wu Mai (Shanghai), Guo Zongxie (Wuchang), Liu Luming (Hankou), Huang Rongchang (Ningbo), Hu Zhen (Zhenjiang), Wang Chaogan and Liu Yifang (Capital). A quorum was met. The meeting was announced at 10:00 AM, and Liu Luming was publicly elected as chairman, and Hu Zhen as recorder. In addition to reporting various matters, the following major cases were resolved: (1) Regarding the issue of how to maintain the finances of the "Law Studies Journal" publishing house, it was resolved to allocate 300 yuan from the pledged additional donations from the Shanghai, Zhenjiang, and Huai'an three chambers to meet urgent needs, and to quickly organize a board of directors to plan for long-term sustainability. (2) Regarding the issue of differing opinions among various associations regarding the method of collecting additional donations, it was resolved to temporarily send letters to each association separately based on their responses, urging them to collect donations according to their specific circumstances to meet needs, and to discuss how to standardize the process at the next general meeting. (3) Regarding the need for a substantial amount of funds for the Association to manage the journal and expand publicity, and the need to implement a budget and final accounting system, it was resolved to hand it over to the Standing Committee for handling. (4) Regarding the request from Li Xuzhang of Hubei and others to forward to the Ministry for review of the alleged dereliction of duty of Zhang Fujia, President of the Hubei High Court, it was resolved to reply that it was not convenient to intervene. (5) Regarding how to prepare for the next representative conference, it was resolved to notify Hangzhou County to take responsibility for handling it according to the conference agenda. (6) On the motion of Director Wu Mai that a column should be opened in the "Law Studies Journal" to provide faithful and fair criticism of all judicial matters to promote the integrity of the rule of law and the rectification of discipline, it was resolved to inform Director Li to handle it accordingly. (7) On the motion of Director Wu Mai that the Association should formally advise the British Minister Sir Miles Lampson against gradually abandoning extraterritoriality, and awaken him to the matter, it was resolved to do so, to task Director Wu with drafting, and to submit it to the Standing Committee for review and issuance. (8) Standing Committee Member Liu Luming moved to resign as Chairman of the "Law Studies Journal" publishing house. It was resolved that since it had been decided by the general meeting, the Executive Committee had no power to accept it, and Liu Luming was still requested to continue his efforts. The meeting adjourned at 7:00 PM, and a public banquet was held within the venue.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Secret Agent Continuously Solves Kidnapping Cases The Fengjing Township in this county is located at the intersection of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces and borders Jinshan and Qingpu. The numerous waterways make it a den for bandits. Kidnapping cases occur from time to time. In the case of Yin Xietai's kidnapped child in Jiaodiao Bay, the secret agent Yang Shijie of the Military Police Inspection Office captured the bandit woman Wu Lushi in Shanghai. After recovering the kidnapped child, the secret agent interrogated her, and she confessed that a bandit named Shen A'san was still hiding in Shanghai. On the 4th, he led secret agents Tang Shuqin, Lu Shounan, and Shen Shoulin to Shanghai and arrested the bandit Shen in Fu'an Lane, Qipu Road. He also transported the kidnapped Shen women and two young children back to Songjiang by the second shift train. After interrogation, it was learned that Shen A'san was the duck herder Shen A'san from Shenjiabang. He was the mastermind behind every kidnapping case near Fengjing. According to his confession, on the 18th of last month, he kidnapped Shen Renru from Nansugang, Shihudang. The next day, the kidnapped victim escaped due to the guard falling asleep. He then went to Bushi Village and kidnapped a Luo boy (nine years old) and returned. According to the Shen woman, she was kidnapped and did not know the details. The secret agent also captured Xie Yunlian, who was involved in the kidnapping case, in Xinzhen, Fengjing. He confessed that on February 13th, he and his accomplice Lu Jinzhou kidnapped the son of Zhu Xinlong from Shangnanbang. Lu brought him to my house, and I received 26.5 yuan. In early May, I and Jia Zixiang delivered three guns to a bandit nearby. On the same day, in the Shijing area, he captured Shen Yin'an, a bandit who rowed the boat for Taibao A'shu. According to his confession, he disembarked at Bainiudang. He also discovered an abandoned boat left by the bandits in Jiangjiabang and took it back to the office for investigation. Yesterday (the 6th), Agent Yang, based on a tip, immediately led agents to Shanghai. He arrested Tao Yunsheng, nicknamed A'pi, in a smoking den in the French Concession, who had repeatedly committed kidnapping cases. The kidnapped victims of Wanliangjing were hidden in South Chengdu Road. He arrested Qian Longxiu, the bandit guarding the hostages, and rescued Shen Genbu's grandson A'shui (six years old) and Chu Jinkui's son A'xiao (eight years old). Both children, along with the two bandits, were taken back by train that night. The results of the interrogation will be used to search for guns in a certain place and to hunt down the remaining bandits. The above captured bandits will be sent to the county government tomorrow for interrogation.

Suzhou

Large Number of Refugees Passing Through Yesterday (the 7th), more than 300 refugees arrived in Suzhou from Kunshan, passing through Waikuatang and then heading towards Wujiang.

High Court Orders Counties to Guard Against Prisoners The President of the High Court, Lin, stated that recently, reactionary elements have frequently engaged in subversive activities. In all county prisons, communist criminals are mixed in with ordinary prisoners, and the number of escaped prisoners is increasing every month. Given the current unsettled situation, counties should be ordered to be vigilant at all times. Therefore, yesterday (the 7th), he specifically ordered the wardens and prison guards of all counties to be vigilant to avoid negligence.

High Court Thoroughly Investigates Sun Zuji's Bribery Case Former Wuxi County Magistrate Sun Zuji, upon leaving office, allegedly bribed prison guards to release prisoners, leading citizens such as Zhang Tong of the county to submit petitions to the High Court and the Provincial Government, requesting a thorough investigation. Yesterday, the High Court Prosecutor's Office replied that the Wuxi County District Court Prosecutor's Office has been ordered to investigate and handle Sun Zuji's bribery and release of prisoners according to the law.

Wuxi

Continued News of Lake Bandits Robbing Two Steamers Further news indicates that the Zhaoshangju's Xinjiangcheng steamer and the Yangxian Company's Guoshan steamer were robbed by bandits on the way from Liuyang to Wuxi at Jiulikou (also known as Penglikou) the other day. Thirteen men and women were kidnapped as hostages. That night, the two steamers were released. Upon receiving the report, Wang Yunwu, the head of the Yixing Chamber of Commerce branch, immediately led members of the Chamber of Commerce and the militia to cooperate with the garrison troops and pursue the bandits by steamer. By noon, they pursued them to Zhukui Bridge and learned that the bandits had dispersed in all directions, with only a few remaining in the mountains. The kidnapped men and women were also being watched. Chief Wang immediately led the militia members to search the mountains and engaged the bandits. The two sides opened fire for half an hour. The bandits, unable to withstand the attack, abandoned the hostages and fled over the mountains, scattering in all directions. The pursuit continued to Linghukou, where the borders of Jiangsu and Zhejiang meet, where they boarded the bandit ship moored there and fled into the lake. Chief Wang rescued the kidnapped men and women.

Sixteen Silk Factories in Wuxi Close The silk reeling industry in Wuxi has not yet achieved its goal of opposing public weighing. The silk market is sluggish, and the factories are losing too much money, making it difficult to maintain operations. After a meeting of all the industry, it was decided to suspend operations uniformly, following the example of Shanghai. The other day was the abolished Mid-Autumn Festival, and the factories still closed down as usual. Starting yesterday, most factories have already closed down. Some factories have had to clear their inventory at a painful loss due to silk transactions. The following is a list of the closed factories, based on available information: Dafeng (next to Zhang Yuan'an), Yingyi (Beixin Bridge), Didayu (Zhoushanbang), Yifeng (outside Guangfu Gate), Sanxin (Sheqiao Head), Jintai (Nanxiatang), Taifu (Tatangxia), Santai (Pinggang Bridge), Yusheng (Tieshu Bridge), Ruifu (Yanggu Bay), Defeng (Jingou Bridge), Yisheng (Lixin Road), Yonghengfeng (Sheqiao Head), Yongyu (Xinglong Bridge), Zhenyicheng (Qingming Bridge), Yuanfeng (Beixin Bridge). A total of sixteen factories.

Two Robbery Cases Occur in Urban and Rural Areas in One Day Recently, robbery cases have occurred frequently in urban and rural areas of this county, causing great concern about public security. Unexpectedly, two more robbery cases occurred yesterday. The following is a record of the events: (1) Two men from Wujin, Wu Ronggao and Gao Bingsheng, had finished transporting pigs in Suzhou and were returning in their empty pig transport boat yesterday afternoon around 4:00 PM. As they approached the Wudian Bridge near Jingyun City in the Second District of this county, four bandits suddenly called out to swing the boat over. Wu and Gao did not understand their meaning and immediately brought the boat ashore. The bandits jumped onto the boat. Unexpectedly, once inside the small river, the bandits overturned the cabin, robbing the pig transport fee of 18 yuan and fleeing ashore. The incident was immediately reported to the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau, which dispatched police to the countryside and captured two suspects, Xu Genrong and Huang Xinggen, who were taken back to the bureau for interrogation. (2) The home of Gao Rongsheng, a villager from Gaoxiang in the Seventh District (Huai Shang City), was suddenly invaded by more than ten bandits the other night, who broke into the house and searched at will. They robbed 130 yuan in cash, 70-80 pieces of clothing, and gold jewelry worth about 300 yuan. Gao Rongsheng was burned on the arm by the bandits, and Gao's elderly mother was beaten all over with hard firewood sticks. The incident has been reported to the district office for submission to the county government, which has ordered a search.

Jiangyin

Detective Team to Be Disbanded The position of captain of the Jiangyin Detective Team has been held by Huang Bingzhong since he was dismissed for the Hongwan case, then temporarily by Huang Jinbiao, and then again by Wu Shanbao. However, cases of banditry have continued to emerge, and none have been solved. Now, County Magistrate Li has decided to disband the detective team on the 5th, deeming it a waste of public funds.

County Magistrate Strictly Handles Jiang Hong Case Former director of the Relief Institute Jiang Hong, for Ji Hehua, was confirmed by County Magistrate Li as having obtained 5,000 yuan from Ji's parents in the name of the county government, with 3,000 yuan used to purchase guns for the Public Security Bureau and 2,000 yuan used for the Relief Institute's medical clinic, implying fraudulent intent. He has been arrested and detained, and Ji's mother, Sha, has been designated as the plaintiff for a thorough investigation. During the interrogation the other day, Jiang Hong stated that the 5,000 yuan had been approved by County Magistrate Li and that he had only acted as an intermediary, with someone named Mei handling the funds. He claimed that he had not directly received the funds and that Ji's mother had personally come to the city to request the rescue of her son, and that he had no intention of obtaining funds under false pretenses. County Magistrate Li absolutely denied Jiang's statements, stating that he should be dealt with strictly according to the law. The outcome of this case is unknown.

Yangzhou

Detailed Account of Prison Break at Detention Center At 5:10 PM on the 6th, a large number of important criminal defendants escaped from the detention center affiliated with the Jiangdu County Court. The general situation was reported in yesterday's special dispatch column. The following is a detailed account of the prison break: The Yangzhou Detention Center is located inside the Jiangdu County Government compound. Outside the detention center, a squadron of police troops is stationed. The other day, 30 of the more combat-capable troops were transferred to Luyang Lake to suppress bandits, leaving the defense weak. The 6th was the Mid-Autumn Festival, and the escaped prisoners, knowing that there were few defenders and that most of the guards were newly replaced, prepared a large amount of wine and meat and held a public feast for the guards. A few prisoners who had not been shackled accompanied them in heavy drinking, while the rest secretly broke their shackles inside the prison. By the time they had mutually broken free, most of the guards were already drunk. In addition, Chen, the head of the detention center, also went to visit Slender West Lake with relatives and friends because it was the Mid-Autumn Festival, so the situation was uncontrollable once it erupted. When the prisoners broke out, they first used their bed boards as weapons, and upon exiting the prison gate, they seized four quick-firing rifles from the police team's fence and rushed out, overwhelming the county government's gate guards. Two of the gate guards were injured. The escaped prisoners fled mostly through the West Gate (because the county government is close to the West Gate). It is estimated that 59 important prisoners escaped. Later, the brigade, police team, and public security bureau successively recaptured ten prisoners, including Zheng Desheng, Xie Jiangxin, Sheng Qichang, Chen A'san, Xian Yuyuan, Xu Ziming, Wang Xiaoliuzi, Cui Lunhua, Zhou Wenhui, and Zhang Fengkui. Chen Churuo was killed in a firefight at Jimaozhuang outside the West Gate. The rest were not found. After the incident, the city gates were closed, and a temporary curfew was announced. However, many people had left the city to visit scenic spots that day and were mostly stranded outside the city. Chen, the head of the detention center, did not enter the city until this morning.

Also, according to a Suzhou dispatch, the High Court received a telegram from the Jiangdu County Court yesterday (the 7th) stating that 56 prisoners escaped from the court's detention center at Shenshi on the 6th. One prisoner was killed on the spot, and eight were captured. President Lin, upon receiving the telegram, immediately dispatched judicial commissioner Gu Douyin to thoroughly investigate and report. It is also said that the reason for the escape of prisoners from the Jiangdu County Court detention center was that the 6th was the Mid-Autumn Festival, and the guards were somewhat negligent, which led to the incident.

Nantong

Li Mingyang Cables to Investigate Surrendered Bandits and Communists In the past month, many Wang bandits and communists in Tongzhou, Rudong, Taixing, and Haian counties have surrendered to the government troops. Rosters are being compiled and submitted to the province for verification. Li Mingyang has cabled from Yancheng, ordering the county magistrates to quickly investigate and report.

Methods for Harvesting Cotton in the Huainan Reclamation Area The Huainan coastal reclamation area has been occupied by large groups of sea bandits, causing employees to flee and making it impossible to harvest cotton. Now, Shen Guanxi's gang has been driven back by the provincial security regiment. Representatives from various districts gathered in Tongcheng to discuss methods for harvesting cotton and resolved to quickly organize a joint militia to protect the tenant farmers in harvesting cotton. A telegram was also sent to the provincial government appealing for assistance. The Civil Affairs Department ordered Xiong Yanghe, the police captain of Funing County, to dispatch troops to assist. Employees and tenants of various companies in Tongcheng have successively gone to the Yanfu reclamation area.

Implementing Rural Pacification in Bandit Areas The areas of Nantong with the deepest banditry, such as Siyu and Pingchao, have been approved by the county government to implement rural pacification, with a period of three months. The Rural Pacification Bureau is attached to the county government, with the county magistrate and the head of the Public Security Bureau as the director and deputy director, respectively. Below them is a rural pacification director, without the establishment of additional departments.

Huzhou

Large Numbers of Refugees Disturb Shanlian and Shichong In Shanlian Town, Wuxing County, Huzhou, over four hundred refugees suddenly arrived, claiming to be from Baoqing County, Henan, in a very miserable state. Led by their representative, Li Zhonghan, they walked from Lianshi to Shanlian and resided in the Xida Temple in the town. The back of the temple is the site of the Shanlian Elementary School in the Fourth District of Wuxing County. After the refugees arrived in Shanlian, only a local police officer was able to manage them, causing the town's shops and the school site to be disrupted. The next day, the refugees left Shanlian and passed through Shichong, staying overnight in the Taijun Temple in the village. They then went out to collect firewood and forcefully took taro, chickens, ducks, and other items from the villagers. Any resistance resulted in violence, causing unrest among the nearby residents. It is reported that the wealthy Shen family in the East Village of Shanlian was invaded by the refugees the other day, who searched the inner rooms and robbed cash, jewelry, clothing, and other items worth no less than 2,000 yuan. Afterward, Shen requested the town's militia to pursue them, but due to the small number of militiamen, they feared being outnumbered and dared not pursue.

Pinghu

Sea Bandit Li Qihe Executed by Firing Squad Li Qihe, alias Li Shunhai, alias Li Lao Zhu (from Linhai), 26 years old, who had previously robbed merchant ships in the waters of Zhapu and was captured and sent to the county, was sentenced to death by the county government due to the severity of his crimes and the sentence was submitted to the province for approval. On the 6th, a telegram was received from the province approving the execution by firing squad. The execution was carried out by police dispatched by the county government at the Wanchang School Grounds outside the South Gate at 1:00 PM.

Jiaxing

Land Bandit Commander Ying Mentioned to He Qian Changxing Militia Commander Zhang Minggao, when ordered to suppress bandits last year, actually led his troops with weapons into Taihu Lake and joined the bandits. The provincial government had issued a reward for his arrest. Zhang was residing in Shanghai. The Jiangsu Water Police Third District Office learned of this and dispatched troops to Shanghai to cooperate with the French Concession police in capturing the bandit. He was sent to the district office for investigation. Hang Yi, the Jiahu Bandit Suppression Commander, stated that the bandit had disrupted the Zhejiang border in several cases and prepared a document to dispatch Adjutant Zhang Lianfeng to lead a squad to Suzhou to retrieve the bandit from the Water Police Third District Office and bring him back to He, where he is being held at the Bandit Suppression Command for further investigation.

Xiaoshan

Economic Oppression Leads to Double Suicide In Zhuangjia Village outside the South Gate of Xiaoshan, there was a man named Lu Xiuhong, who made a living as a small vendor. He lived with only his elderly wife and had no children. In recent years, rice and firewood have become expensive, making it difficult to make a living. He borrowed money from all sides, increasing his debt. The recent festival season also brought many debt collectors, and Lu was unable to cope. He conceived a desperate plan. Last night (the 5th), Lu Xiuhong and his wife both hanged themselves. Neighbors only found out this morning, and it was too late to save them.

Shops' Festival Accounts Collected Less This year, the provincial government stipulated that the 9th of May, September, and December were the deadline for shops to collect accounts. However, shops in Xiaoshan have not changed their old habits and continue to use the Mid-Autumn Festival season to collect accounts from debtors. However, this year's festival accounts were very meager. It is estimated that the shops collected less than half of the accounts owed.

Request to Allocate Dike Engineering Fees The Xiaoshan County Government reported to the Construction Department that the dike project in the Hechangda Third Township is extremely important and cannot be delayed any longer. It requested the transfer of a letter to the Shatian Bureau requesting the advance allocation of 10,000 yuan in construction funds for use. It is learned that the Construction Department has sent a letter to the Shatian Bureau requesting the advance allocation of 10,000 yuan to meet the urgent need and ordered Xiaoshan County to raise the one-quarter of the expenses to be borne by the three townships within one week for construction use.

Incoming Letter

Letter from Changshu County Government

Respectfully, I recently read the article "Firefight Between Police and Bandits at the Border of Yu and Cheng" in the local correspondence column of your newspaper on October 2nd. It is inconsistent with the facts. Shizhuang belongs to the jurisdiction of Jiangyin and is not at the border with our county. Furthermore, the Jiangyin Fortress Command did not notify our county to dispatch troops to join in the suppression. Such reports may cause misunderstandings among the people and have a great impact on local public security. Please publish a letter to correct this and clarify the facts. Changshu County Government, respectfully, October 4th

Educational News Highlights

Ministry Orders Exemption of Tuition Fees for Students from Shaanxi, Gansu, Suiyuan, and Chahar

The Ministry of Education recently issued another order to the education departments of various provinces, except for the four provinces of Shaanxi, Gansu, Suiyuan, and Chahar (and the education bureaus of Nanjing, Shanghai, Tianjin, and Qingdao), that tuition fees for students from the disaster areas of Shaanxi, Gansu, Suiyuan, and Chahar in all secondary schools should be reduced or exempted as appropriate this academic year. The Ministry of Education had previously issued an order on this matter and is now informing the various departments and bureaus to instruct the schools to pay attention to the matter.

Representatives of Ten Zhejiang Provincial Middle Schools Go to the Province to Demand Outstanding Payments

Zhejiang Provincial No. 10 Middle School has been renovated since the beginning of the semester. The school buildings have been repaired, and a new wireless telephone has been installed for practical training of science students. New fire engines have been purchased to prevent fire alarms. Students are studying diligently, and teachers and staff are doing their best. Both senior and junior high school students have established self-government associations, published weekly and monthly magazines, and organized consumer cooperatives. On the faculty and staff side, book clubs, Party Theory Research Society, soccer teams, tennis teams, and basketball teams have been organized. It has recently been learned that the school has been overdue in receiving provincial funds for four months. Student fees have been used up, and teachers and staff are pawning their belongings to make ends meet. They are working for the public on empty stomachs, which cannot last long. The principal has repeatedly telegraphed the province, but to no avail. It is becoming difficult to cope, and the school is about to run out of funds. Therefore, all teachers and staff held a temporary meeting the other day and resolved to send representatives to the province to demand the outstanding payments. Jin Bixian and Chen Guangzeng were elected as representatives of all teachers and staff to demand the outstanding payments.

Ministry of Education Approves Filing of Board of Directors of Jinling Women's College

Jinling Women's University Changed to College The Ministry of Education previously received a submission from the Nanjing Municipal Education Bureau of the filing forms for the Board of Directors and the school for the private Jinling Women's University and forwarded them for review. Yesterday, the Ministry of Education instructed the Municipal Education Bureau to approve the establishment of the school's Board of Directors and to approve the filing at the same time. However, the name should be changed to the Board of Directors of the Private Jinling Women's College. The unsatisfactory points in the constitution of the Board of Directors should be deleted and revised immediately. The school filing must wait until the Ministry of Education sends someone to inspect it before it can be reviewed and approved.

Hunan Province Re-requests Complete Independence of Education Funding

and Plans for Future Education Changsha Correspondence: After the recent devastation of Hunan Province by the communists, the education community suffered heavy losses. Education funds have been temporarily advocated by the government. Salt tax revenue has decreased sharply compared to before. Schools that have not been burned down are mostly stationed by troops, and public and private property has been damaged in countless numbers. Although half a month's funding has been distributed at the request of people in the education community and schools have reopened one after another, there is no guarantee for previous arrears and future funding given the current state of the government. The reason for this recurring phenomenon is that education funding is not completely independent. Therefore, the Provincial Education Association convened an executive committee meeting at 4:00 PM on the 1st. More than ten people, including Hu Yiru, attended. Fang Kegang chaired the meeting, reported the purpose of the meeting, and then discussed various proposals below: (1) How should we request the government to maintain the original plan for the complete independence of education funding in this period? It was resolved to send a letter to the Education Department, asking them to be responsible for negotiating with the salt transport bureau to request that the education funding under the salt tax item for July, August, and September be allocated in full to the Education Funding Guarantee Committee, and to request the government to expedite the issuance of the funding for July, August, and September according to the original budget. If the provincial treasury does not have enough to issue, please withdraw a portion from the deposit item of the Education Funding Guarantee Committee for temporary advance payment. (2) Please ask the Education Department to revise the charter of the Education Funding Management Committee to seek complete independence. It was resolved to submit a special proposal to the Education Department for implementation. (3) How should post-disaster education be planned and carried out? It was resolved: (A) To submit a report to the Education Department to announce the post-disaster education facility plan. (B) To publish notices soliciting opinions from education institutions and school administrators in various cities. (C) To designate executive committee members of the association to be responsible for drafting the following education plans: (1) Primary education, (2) Secondary education, (3) Vocational education, (4) Normal education, (5) Public education. (6) Strengthen the work of eliminating communists. It was resolved to ask the secretary-general to draft a plan and submit it to the executive committee for approval and implementation. (5) Please submit a report to the provincial government to repair Zhongshan Hall in advance to avoid greater losses over time. It was resolved to send a document to the Education Department today requesting the provincial government to repair it in advance. (6) The communists have looted the country, and the National Government has specially issued 100,000 yuan in national currency to comfort the people of Changsha. Our education community has suffered huge losses. How should we request the government to distribute it quickly and evenly? It was resolved to consult with the city chamber of commerce in advance to formulate a plan and then negotiate with the Provincial Relief Committee. (7) Send a letter to the charity association requesting the allocation of a portion of funds to maintain post-education funding. It was resolved to pass the motion as is. The meeting adjourned.

Shandong Provincial Government Raises Funds for Studying Abroad

Jinan Quick News: He Siyuan, member of the Shandong Provincial Government and Director of the Education Department, stated that Shandong owes a huge amount of funding for studying abroad in the East and the West. As of the end of September, it had reached 147,892.3 yuan and urgently needs to be raised as soon as possible to support the scholars studying abroad. Therefore, he submitted a detailed list of the funding for studying abroad in the East and the West to the sixth political affairs meeting of the provincial government for discussion. It was resolved to order the finance department to allocate funds as appropriate and handle the procedures according to previous practice. The proposal is recorded below. Report from the Secretariat: The Education Department submitted a list of outstanding funding for studying abroad in the East and the West for review. How should it be handled? Please make a public decision. The Education Department reported that it had been ordered to investigate and report the amount of funding owed to students studying abroad. It has been found that as of the end of September of this year, a total of 147,892.3 yuan in national currency is owed for studying abroad in the East and the West. A list and inventory are attached for review. In addition, the various amounts listed in the table are calculated based on recent market prices. Recently, the value of gold coins in various countries has fluctuated, and if there is insufficient funding during the remittance, a request will be submitted for review and supplement. As for the remittance fee, because it fluctuates with the price of gold, it is impossible to predict in advance. It is proposed that when allocating funding for studying abroad, it should be calculated according to the market price and submitted for approval. How should it be handled? Please make a public decision. Attached is a list and inventory (omitted).

Annual Meeting of the China Cooperative Society

To Open in Hangzhou the Day After Tomorrow

The second annual meeting of the China Cooperative Society will be held in Hangzhou, Zhejiang, starting on the 9th of this month, as previously reported. The following is further information received:

Submitted Papers: Wang Shiying's "The Foundation for Success in Agricultural Cooperation," Shou Miancheng's "Cooperatives and Economic Rationalization," and Wu Yuzhang's "The Cooperative View of Profit."

Welcome to Auditors: The Society has received many letters from various sectors requesting to attend as auditors, and all have been answered individually. These include Chen Denghao and He Weileng, representatives from the Fujian Cooperative Society and the Consumer Association; Zeng Wanjun, a promoter of cooperative enterprises in Jiashan; and Huang Danzai, Weng Dazao, Wang Zhenhuan, and Qiu Hongqing from Fudan University. The Society welcomes comrades who are interested in cooperation to request to audit.

Public Lectures: The Society has agreed to requests from various institutions in Hangzhou to give public lectures, including the Autonomous Training School, the Police Academy, the Provincial Women's Sericulture Training Institute, the Reformatory, the Detention Personnel Training Institute, and Hongdao Girls' School. The radio station also plans to use radio to broadcast speeches on cooperation.

Re-election of the Hangzhou Branch of the China Economic Society

Jin Runquan Elected President

The Hangzhou Branch of the China Economic Society has made significant progress since its establishment last year. It holds monthly dinners, convened in rotation by its members, to foster connections. Any matters for discussion are brought up and decided upon at the dinner meetings. On the afternoon of the other day at 2:00 PM, the fifth dinner meeting was held, hosted by members Wang Zhuzhai, Wang Xiangquan, and Jin Runquan. Eighteen people attended, including Cheng Zhenji, Xu Xinggong, Jin Runquan, Zhao Wenrui, Zheng Zhilian, Wang Yongxin, Li Pei'en, Xu Sipei, Wu E, Wang Xiangquan, Wang Zhuzhai, Wei Songtang, Jiang Yuanxin, Huo Baoshu, Ma Yinchu, Han Zude, Wu Juenong, and Chen Qilu. The dinner was held at the Jin residence in Youyi Lane. At the meeting, officers were re-elected. The officers, including the president, vice president, secretary, and treasurer, are re-elected annually. The previous president was Qian Xinzhi, the vice president was Wei Songtang, and the secretary and treasurer was Wang Yongxin. Their terms had reached one year and were due for re-election. The re-election results from last night showed that Jin Runquan received the most votes and was elected as president, Jiang Yuanxin was elected as vice president, and Wang Yongxin was re-elected as secretary and treasurer. After the election, discussions were held on the Fund Society and other society affairs. The meeting concluded at over 10:00 PM, with everyone in good spirits.

Specialist from the Nanjing Public Education Hall in Beijing to Investigate

The Ministry of Education, based on the Jiangsu Provincial Nanjing Public Education Hall's assignment of Wang Ziyun as a specialist in social education investigation stationed in France, requested the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to instruct the embassy in France to provide detailed guidance. The Ministry of Education has now consulted the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to instruct the embassy in France to provide guidance and facilitate the investigation.

Chen Bulei Summoned to the Front Lines

Chen Bulei, a member of the Zhejiang Provincial Government and Director of the Education Department, received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek a few days ago, instructing him to go to the front lines to discuss important matters. Upon receiving the telegram, Chen left Hangzhou for Beijing on the same day, heading north and then to Henan Province to meet with Chiang.

Chuansha Public Primary School Ordered to Become an Experimental Primary School

The Chuansha County Public Primary School has a long history and outstanding achievements. Since Mr. Lu Rong'an took over as principal last year, the school has made even greater progress. Recently, the Education Department, based on the inspection report of the Provincial Superintendent, considered the school to be a model primary school in the Pudong area due to its large scale and excellent management. It instructed the Education Bureau to transform the school into an experimental primary school. Upon receiving the order, the Education Bureau immediately complied and notified the school. It is reported that Principal Lu is now planning everything in preparation for the reorganization.

Local News

City Education Bureau Orders All Educational Institutions in the City to Enthusiastically Celebrate National Day

The Shanghai City Education Bureau issued three instructions to all schools, public education halls, and public school gardens yesterday regarding the enthusiastic celebration of National Day: (Instruction to Municipal and Private Schools at All Levels) "The National Day celebration of this year is approaching, and all schools in the city should celebrate it together. In addition to participating in celebrations organized by various sectors, each school should convene all teachers and students at 8:00 AM on that day to hold a flag-raising ceremony and a National Day celebration meeting. In addition to separate instructions, a copy of the order of events is urgently issued for the schools to follow." "Order of Events for the Commemoration Meeting": (1) Opening of the meeting; (2) Singing the Party song; (3) Paying the highest respects to the national flag and the Party flag; (4) The chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will; (5) Silent tribute; (6) The chairman's report; (7) Speeches; (8) Adjournment. "Order of Events for the Flag-Raising Ceremony": (1) Entering in single file; (2) Standing at attention; (3) Playing music; (4) Singing the Party song; (5) Raising the flag; (6) Firing cannons; (7) Paying the highest respects to the national flag; (8) Playing music; (9) Ceremony concludes. (Instruction to the Municipal Simple Public Education Hall) "National Day commemoration is an important event for the Republic of China, and all citizens should celebrate it to promote national glory. The hall, as a public education institution, is responsible for guiding the public. On the Double Tenth Day, it should gather nearby residents to hold a celebration meeting and add a recreational event as entertainment to inspire the public's sense of celebration. This is of utmost importance." (Instruction to the Directors of the First and Second Municipal Public School Gardens) "The academic calendar for this year stipulates that all primary and secondary schools should have a holiday and hold meetings to celebrate National Day on October 10th. Since this day is a holiday, the public school garden should be open all day for students to enter and enjoy themselves. In addition to separate instructions, this order is hereby issued for the director to comply with and implement." End of order.

Shanghai South Education Association to Hold General Meeting Today

The Shanghai South District Municipal Education Association previously decided to hold a general meeting of members at Wantzhu Primary School at 7:00 PM on October 8th. All members have been notified, and the Party Department and the Education Bureau will send personnel to provide guidance. Labor University Students Petition in Beijing

Hubei Province Holds Sports Competition

Huang Jianzhong, Director of the Education Department of Hubei Province, initiated sports competitions for various schools, emphasizing practicality. The following is a record of his instructions and methods:

Instructions: It is noted that sports competitions should not focus on form but on spirit, and not on spirit but on universality. Often, schools hold sports meets with extravagance and waste of money, with only selected athletes participating in running and jumping, completely losing the meaning of sports, and wasting the spirit and time of learning. Thinking of this, I am deeply saddened. The intention of this provincial student sports competition is to eliminate the accumulated bad habits of the past and establish a more progressive method. All extravagance that easily leads to extra classes and waste is eliminated, and exercises that are not suitable for the season or physiology are generally discarded. Emphasis is placed on group competitions, striving to make young students tend towards group discipline in order to eliminate the accumulated ills of abnormal development and cultivate the spirit of loving the group and cooperating. Consider the promotion of sports education to achieve universality. In addition to separate instructions, all schools should first promote universal sports education, group disciplinary action, and, in particular, adhere to the spirit of sports in order to develop education and participate in this competition as much as possible. This is of utmost importance. Attached is one copy of the Hubei Provincial Student Sports Competition regulations and one copy of the group teaching materials.

Regulations: The key points of the competition regulations are recorded below. All provincial schools at all levels and private schools that have been registered can participate in the competition. The competition is divided into the following groups according to the nature and level of the school: Group A University and Specialty Group, Group B High School Group, Group C Junior High School Group, Group D Girls' Group (middle school girls), and Group E Primary School Group (co-ed gymnastics group). The competition events are stipulated as follows: Group A Gymnastics, (1) Freehand Exercises, (2) Military Exercises, (3) Boy Scout Performance, Group B Ball Sports (1) Soccer (2) Basketball (3) Mini-Soccer (4) Volleyball (5) Baseball (6) Tennis. When participating in the competition, schools will generally send representatives to participate in preliminary competitions in accordance with the time, location, and order of competing schools determined in the preliminary schedule. At the end of the preliminary competition, a final competition will be held on a scheduled basis. The final competition will be the Hubei Provincial Student Sports Competition, which must be held no later than November 1st. Therefore, all preliminary competitions should be completed before November 5th.

Establishment of the All-Japan Judo Selection Tournament

Spare No Effort to Promote National Arts

Large-Scale Organized Competition

Tokyo Correspondence (Observers attribute the rapid progress of sports in Japan in recent years to the excellent organization of sports associations. Various sports have nationally unified organizations to provide scientific guidance and large-scale competitions. However, it is inexplicable that judo, a branch of national arts that has always been popular in society, only recently, through the efforts of various parties, has the organization of the All-Japan Judo Selection Tournament. The charter of the association is recorded below:

(Purpose) To crack down on various illegal judo competitions nationwide and hold the All-Japan Selection Tournament. (Tournament Date) Held annually in Tokyo, this year scheduled for November 15th and 16th at the Meiji Jingu Outer Garden Sumo Arena. (Officers) One president, one chairman, directors responsible for all association affairs, councilors to plan all important association affairs, committee members to implement all association affairs, and advisors to provide advice to the chairman. (Districts) The country is divided into personnel selection districts. (Types of Athletes) Those who are engaged in judo instruction and teach judo are professional athletes; those who practice judo as an amateur sport and for self-cultivation are general athletes. (Athlete Classes) Those aged 20 to 30 are early-stage adult athletes; those aged 30 to 38 are late-stage adult athletes; those aged 38 to 44 are early-stage senior athletes; and those aged 44 and above are late-stage senior athletes. (Selection Method) District competitions are held annually first, and each district selects one athlete of each class and one alternate athlete to represent them at the national tournament. The national tournament selects one athlete from each class. (Awards) (1) Winners of each class in the national competition will be given a certificate as the All-Japan Judo Selection Tournament holder and an award plaque. (1) Winners of each class in each district will be given a certificate as the District Selection Tournament holder and an award plaque. (1) Second place winners of each class in each district will be given a certificate. (Expenses) The travel expenses and accommodation fees in Tokyo for athletes selected from districts to participate in the tournament will be subsidized by the association by 30%. The expenses of alternate athletes and supervisors from districts will be borne by the districts.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Seafarer

Barber (teaching a new apprentice): "In our business, the first thing is to be polite. When you see a customer, always put on a smiling face and say a few words to compliment him."

Apprentice: "Master, I can do that. But if I see a bald customer, how should I compliment him?"

Barber: "You say, 'Sir, your hair is too long. Would you like a trim?'"

Police officer (sees a child crying by the river): "Little friend, what's wrong?"

Child (still crying, pointing to the middle of the river): "My brother—"

Police officer (interrupting, jumps into the river. After a while) brings up a hat. "What's this? Your brother is not in the river."

Child: "My brother wasn't originally there. He threw my hat into the river and ran away. I hadn't finished speaking. Why are you in such a hurry?"

Lecturer (raising his head, speaking eloquently) suddenly stops, seeing a young man next to him yawning. "Hey, comrade, you're tired of listening to such an energetic lecture?"

Young man: "I'm not listening. Look around, the audience has already left. I'm just waiting for you to finish so I can sweep the floor, wipe the table, and lock the door."

Nostalgic Notes from Zhu'an

— Da Ke

The golden wind rises suddenly, and the jade dew is slightly scattered. Among the clumps of osmanthus trees, there are melancholy thoughts. Within three hundred li, the most famous place for osmanthus trees is Hangzhou's Manjuelong and my Jiahe's Zhuan. Manjuelong is known for its abundance, and Zhuan for its antiquity. Both are scenic spots in fragrant forests. Zhuan is located about ten li southeast of Jiahe City. Taking a boat from Xuan Gong Bridge, passing Nanhus, and along Changshuitang, one can reach it after about a meal's time. Twin osmanthus trees stand tall by the eaves. One is over two zhang tall, and the other is over one zhang tall. Both are hundreds of years old. Some say they were planted by Zhu Wenge Gong of the Ming Dynasty. After checking the Baoshu Ting Collection, there is no record of this. It is probably untraceable. The nunnery worships Garan. The nuns who run it are scattered due to wars and disasters. The halls are also about to collapse. Jin Xiangyan of the village donated funds to repair it, and it was restored to its former glory. In the mid-autumn of the year Wuchen, I, together with Xiangyan, Guo Heting and the Qiting brothers, invited Zhu Qiangcun Yanzhang, Liu Zuquan Cibifu and his son, Yao Yuqin, Yan Qizhou, and other gentlemen to take a boat trip. At that time, Lin Tiezun was in charge of the salt tax in Jiahe, and he was happy to come when he heard about it. Ten people, hosts and guests, lingered all day. Heting hand-painted a map of Zhuan's visit to the osmanthus trees to record the footprints. Xiangyan and others composed poems and lyrics, which were inscribed on the back of the scroll. They boasted of it as a gathering of elegance at the time. Looking back at the west wind, three years have passed in a hurry. Xiangyan passed away last winter. I am also running around for food and clothing, with no interest. Occasionally, I open the old map and feel sad. Among the inscriptions in the map, Qiangweng was the first to write, followed by Tie Lao. The two gentlemen are contemporary Zhou Jiang, and their reputation as masters of lyrics is well-established. I am not modest, and I also composed a tune of Osmanthus Branch Fragrance. Qiangzhang said it was like Wang Banshan's work. The predecessors' praise is deeply ashamed. It is attached here to serve as a call from the hermits of Xiaoshan. Qiangweng's Good Things Close says, "Leaving the world, Guanghan immortals, the fragrant world opens another toad door. Outside the constant sands robbery, compare the moon to the ancient pine on the plate. (Note: At Tiancheng Temple on Panshan) The colored body does not hinder being covered in yellow silk, and crushed gold cloth covers the ground. Even if the poor eaves are exhausted, offer bamboo shoots and axes." Tie Weng's Night Flying Magpie says, "Heavenly fragrance degrees Yun Yun, golden millet piled into heaps of flowers and leaves surging beside the lotus platform. Swaying and scattered Guanghan shadow, Juan Juan Chan mirror deeply open. Kou Dian baskets seem to carry the cover, it is expected to push the southern room to hide. Broken dreams come back for the first time, and after the bell sounds, accompany Vimalakirti for a hundred years of cold ashes. Clear tears from the dew plate disappear, the old fragrant forest of golden medicine. The same as artemisia. The wind outside the red gauze is full of fragrance, and no dust reaches it. Ying Luo lingers. Zhi Qiong has been gone for a long time, and the forehead is yellow with autumn cups. The meaning of osmanthus and Zen, wordless meeting, the moon land comes again." My Osmanthus Branch Fragrance says, "Returning with embrace, taking advantage of maple leaves and reed flowers, the lake is early in autumn. Hearing that the fragrance of osmanthus has not yet arrived, Zen mind is easily annoyed. The Garan is desolate, the bells and fish are cold, and the osmanthus trees are good. After the robbery of the Garden, gold covers the ground, who will sweep it. Don't talk about the literary talent of Huainan, count the joys and sorrows, generally sloppy. Where the lyricists were drunk that day, who can point it out. The yellow-haired people have been gone for years, and the catkins and slanting sun, white-haired old woman. Can't climb and take it. Laugh at me in the wind, the hair is about to grow old.

A Humorous Anecdote of Mistakenly Swapping Vegetarian and Meat Braided Cords

— 斅厂

There was a man named Han in Pingyao who still wore a braid. One year on New Year's Eve, Han went to a barber shop nearby for a haircut. After it was finished, he went home to sleep. When he got into bed and coiled his braid, he suddenly realized that his black braided cord had been replaced with a white one. He was very angry and rushed to the barber shop to question them. The barber was the shop owner, Jin. Jin was stunned when questioned, but then he realized that the white braided cord belonged to another customer who was there at the time. Jin had mistakenly tied the white braided cord onto Han's braid because he was tired late at night. When Han returned, the other customer was still getting his hair cut in the shop. Jin, realizing his mistake, quickly apologized to Han and replaced it with the original. Han was furious and said that he had to guarantee his good luck for the coming year. After some persuasion from others, he reluctantly went home. Unexpectedly, by coincidence, a few days earlier, Han's father had suddenly passed away. Han thought that this misfortune was due to the mistaken white braided cord from last year. Therefore, he was uncontrollably angry and gathered many people, intending to negotiate with the barber shop. A neighbor, Song, learned about this and came out to dissuade him, and Han finally stopped. It was indeed a coincidence and an amusing story.

Supplement to a Scene of Reunion and Separation of Famous Actors

— 澤丞

Previously, a report mentioned the famous actor Wang Yunfang breaking away from his adoptive father. His life story, as reported in various newspapers and magazines, still felt vague, or detailed but not true. Now, based on what I know, I will supplement it to be more accurate. Initially, he experienced chaos in his youth. The disaster he encountered was neither natural nor man-made, but due to discord between father-in-law and son-in-law, resulting in a loss of contact. This led to wandering, barely escaping death, and encountering both tragedy and wonder. Please take this as a factual account to share with readers.

Distinguished Family: Yunfang was from a prominent family in Jintan. His grandfather, Shouqin, was a successful candidate in the imperial examination in the year of Bingzi and served as the head of Dongchang Prefecture in Shandong. His father, Bichang, also served as an official in Shandong. He was known for his integrity and good governance wherever he went. When he retired and returned to his hometown, hundreds of people welcomed him, resembling the style of the two Shu who retired in the past.

Raised by Maternal Relatives: Yunfang lost his mother at the age of four. His father, feeling unable to raise him well, sent him to his maternal uncle's family in Jinan. His maternal grandmother doted on him, and his maternal grandfather taught him to read. He was naturally intelligent, and by the age of nine, he was proficient in literature and art.

Beaten and Abused: Later, his maternal grandmother passed away, and her successor was fierce and unreasonable. He was subjected to beatings, stabbings, and all kinds of abuse. Cold and hunger were common occurrences. He had no choice but to flee. His maternal family also moved soon after. At that time, his father was poor and out of contact, so he simply ignored him.

Unusual Flute Sound: After fleeing, he wandered the streets. During the day, he pretended to be a storyteller, playing the flute in the market. At night, he used the clock tower in the town as a place to rest. His childhood was spent in poverty, to this extent. However, his intelligence was unmatched.

Unstable Fosterage: There was a Qiu who worked as a salt carrier. He pitied Yunfang's refined appearance and took him in as an adoptive son, adopting the surname Qiu and changing his name to Jianzhou. After living there for more than a month, they were ultimately incompatible, and Qiu drove him away again.

Piaomu Feeds Han Xin: It was the end of the year, and he was suffering from hunger and cold. He was sleeping alone on a millstone when two women came to work, grinding. They took pity on him as a descendant of nobility and took him home, clothing and feeding him. This was not unlike Piaomu of that year.

Imprisoned by Bandits: One day, he suddenly encountered Qiu on the road and followed him to Cao County. He was captured when bandits attacked Cao City. He was in the midst of gunfire every day (the scar on his leg is still there). After several months, he managed to escape to Jinan.

Studying at the Society: At that time, the Shandong Province established the Easy Customs Society, which recruited talented young people, providing general education as well as teaching opera. Yunfang joined. He graduated after six years, repeatedly winning championships. He was already eighteen years old.

Cao Qiu Becomes Famous: From there, he traveled north to Beijing and studied under Wang Yaoqing, making further progress. He was introduced by Sun Jun Xiaolin to the Gong Stage and Tianchan Stage in Shanghai. His fame grew, all thanks to Sun Jun's promotion.

Recognizing His Son with a Unique Pill: Once he became famous, newspapers competed to report his anecdotes. It wasn't until the spring of this year that his father read the newspaper and came to Shanghai to find his son. They talked and found that many things matched, especially the hidden story of the unique pill, which served as irrefutable proof. Unable to contain their grief and joy, the scene of the reunion of flesh and blood was realized.

"Wild Orchids" Film Review

— 欣俯

"Wild Orchids" starring Greta Garbo, tells the story of an American couple traveling to Java. On their trip, they encounter a Javanese prince and his concubine, Mayna, who pretends to befriend the husband while secretly trying to seduce him. When her secret affair is discovered, she becomes enraged and attempts to kill the prince during a tiger hunt. Fortunately, he is saved in time. The wife then criticizes her husband for being so cruel. The husband believes that his wife has fallen in love with the prince and angrily returns home alone. But when he boards the train, he sees that his wife is already waiting for him in the compartment. It is only then that the wife's true feelings are revealed. The plot is full of twists and turns, far beyond what the audience can imagine.

Ms. Garbo's charming demeanor and artistic talent are already well-known at home and abroad. However, there is one more thing worth mentioning. The women Garbo has portrayed in previous films have often been dissolute and unruly. But in this film, she plays a beautiful and cold young woman who refuses to abandon her elderly husband for the handsome and dashing prince. Her attitude, seemingly affectionate yet indifferent, will captivate even the audience. Garbo is truly versatile.

In terms of background, there are magnificent Javanese palaces and beautiful Javanese landscapes. In terms of interspersed scenes, there are captivating Javanese dances and thrilling tiger attacks, all of which are very interesting to watch. The film is scheduled to premiere at the Paris Grand Theater the day before the Double Tenth Festival.
