Travel Notes from Southeast Asia (61)

— 靈花

On July 14th, Principal Huang Shuitian and Ou Ying gave speeches at his school. That day was the 19th day of the sixth lunar month, the birthday of Guanyin. Master Daojie, Master Wanhui, nuns Zheng Kangmian and Chen Youjia, and others initiated the Guanyin Wan Yuan Meeting at Longhua Temple.

On the 18th, Wang Qiyuan, the manager of the Anxi Association, invited me to move into the Anxi Association. Chairman Lin Gengshen and Chen Liangliang hosted me. On the 20th, Chen Shoujin, the manager of the Yangon newspaper Yunxin Poetry Society, and others invited me to give a lecture at the poetry society. Their society's rules were quite commendable. The society had fewer than a hundred members, but their achievements were remarkable. Their method was to hold a meeting every week, arbitrarily selecting two characters. For example, "Tian Zhou" (Universe) would be used, and dice would be rolled to determine the number of dots, which would then correspond to the nth character in a seven-character line, named the nth chant. This would form a couplet, and each person would create several couplets. For each couplet created, two jiao of silver must be paid. Each volume used pre-printed strips of paper without the author's name. The president would then be publicly elected to evaluate A and B grades. For example, if 30 out of 100 couplets were selected, there would be a reward. Forty couplets would be considered medium selection, and the remaining thirty would be deputy selection. The prize money for the thirty names would come from the two jiao of silver paid by each person for each of the hundred couplets. If a person created five couplets and one was selected, they could break even. This was just one example. There were other methods as well. In general, this method was less rigid, and creating a poem was more interesting, so it lasted for a long time without declining. I saw that there were quite a few valuable couplets created according to this example and greatly appreciated them. This was truly a magnificent view of overseas culture. Everyone invited me to speak. My topic was the Poetry Movement and the Main Points of Life Revolution, describing how China, India, and Greece were all enlightened by poetry. In ancient times, reciting poetry was used for governing. Today, England has a poet laureate. US President Wilson's speech before entering the war stated the power of poets, which people do not know. If the world's politics are to be greatly improved, then politicians must be poets. Therefore, I hope to attract more new members, and it would be even better to attract female poets to join. We can also open a youth division for those aged eight or nine to nineteen. Vernacular poetry can also be added, along with elegant games such as music, Western painting, fine arts, and sports. We can also set up a poetry village. I once started the Juehua Poetry Society in Beiping, wanting to start a poetry village movement, but I did not find a good method. Overseas movements have great prospects. This is truly improving the national flower's literary brilliance. As a result, everyone selected two characters as the next poetry topic and invited me to judge the poems.

On the 23rd, I met again with the secretary of the Theosophical Society, Naganattans. I gave a lecture at the association last time, which was greatly appreciated by everyone. This time, I asked about the association's content and learned that although it was in Myanmar, it was still run by Indians. This gentleman was also an Indian. There was a tacit understanding between China and India in terms of spirit, and they were working together on cultural movements. When I go to India in the future, the association will send someone to wholeheartedly receive me because the association has 15 million people worldwide, and the president is an Indian woman. I was also given a copy of "Awakening" by the vice president, Mrs. Cousing.

Correspondence from Europe (76)

— Liu Haisu

Pilgrimage to Italy Diary

(2) Yu Zhong (C

When the train crossed the border between Italy and France, it was around 3 p.m. We went through the routine procedures of checking passports and luggage. From this point on, the weather gradually became hotter, and everything felt different. The most noticeable difference was the gendarmes wearing Napoleon-style tricorn hats and uniforms at every station. Some of them had fluffy white or black chicken feathers attached to their hats, which were very eye-catching. There were also many beautiful young women coming and going. The wide-brimmed hats made of cicada-wing gauze and the delicate pale yellow jackets were truly stunning. This must be the current popular dress in Italy. The beauty of Italian women is completely different from that of French women. They have strong and lively bodies, breasts that protrude like a 90-degree arc, full and shaking without sagging, resembling Greek and Roman sculptures. It is a kind of aesthetic bewilderment. Straight noses, fluffy and soft hair, cherry-like lips, and two dark eyes full of sparkling light beneath delicate eyebrows all resemble the goddesses in Titian's paintings. They are truly intriguing. Their moving posture and the beauty of their lively and abundant expressions are rare in any Western country.

We arrived in Turin, which marked the end of one stage. After transferring to the train we needed, we ate at the station. The weather was already very hot. The cheerful Italians are always pushing forward, and the crisp sounds coming from their mouths are very pleasant to hear. I have heard people say that the Italian language is light, graceful, crisp, and otherworldly. It is a sacred song praising the gods. The French language is clear and flowing, like elegant social speech in a salon. It is the elegant clear sound of the human world. I have a similar feeling. The train continued to move southeast. All along the way, I saw clusters of lush trees by the road. In some places, very tall and green coconut trees grew, and the ground was full of large cacti. The green of the grass was so green that it seemed oily. Because of this, I felt that I had already tasted the flavor of Southern Europe. As we continued, we traveled for about an hour or two. From near Genoa, the train we were on continued along the coast. This is the Tyrrhenian Sea. Mer Tyrrhenienne

The blue sky of Southern Europe shines on the boundless, calm green sea. The exquisite and elegant old houses along the coast are covered with sea breeze, wrapped in a pleasant atmosphere. As I looked at these places, I thought, Putuo Mountain is not so beautiful, Japan is not so elegant, and Switzerland is not so vast. I think there are few such places in the world. Such majestic mountains and rivers must have soaked into the minds of the Italians and influenced their nature.

Cotton Yarn: An Observation of the Cotton Yarn Market Under Pressure

The Past, Present, and Future: The cotton yarn market seems to have entered a state of stalemate, hovering between 34 and 35 taels. The upward momentum seems insufficient, but a decline is also unlikely. It is extremely difficult to predict the future. The situation in the cotton yarn market was extremely abrupt in the middle of last month. The news of peace in the northern war situation, which had been brewing for several months, gave the weakened market a sudden boost. Within days, the price rose from 47-48 taels to 53-54 taels, a sharp increase. The cotton yarn market had been languishing for a long time due to war and the spread and persistence of banditry. The current rebound of 7-8 taels due to good news about the situation is not considered excessive. However, the interior is plagued by soldiers and bandits, and its vitality is almost exhausted. Furthermore, after last year's poor harvest, current sales have been sluggish. Although the merchants were excited by the news of peace, there was no demand in the interior. However, in view of the expectation of higher prices in the market, they had to make some purchases. This sluggishness in current sales is a manifestation of this phenomenon. Therefore, the maximum transaction volume was only 4,000-5,000 bales. Although a transaction volume of 4,000-5,000 bales is better than the 1,000-2,000 bales in the past, it is still not much in a situation where the market is extremely tired and reacting after a long period of chaos. Moreover, the price of American cotton plummeted from over 11 cents to close to 10 cents. Therefore, the rising trend in the cotton yarn market was hit hard and temporarily stopped. However, a decline seems unlikely in the short term, as the atmosphere of peace and market sentiment will be stimulated. In summary, although the peaceful situation is enough to promote the development of the cotton yarn market, there are still many opposing forces. In other words, the forces driving the market upward are strong, but they have been offset by other factors. Temporarily, the market will likely remain in a state of consolidation, waiting for external forces to determine its rise or fall.

Pessimism About the Future of Raw Cotton

U.S. Cotton Estimates Increase Again… World Consumption Declines

Domestic Cotton Harvests Are Poor… New Cotton Enters the Market in Small Quantities

Foreign Cotton Schools Sell Vigorously… Domestic Cotton Fatigue Becomes More Apparent

The cotton market is in a state of uncertainty. Considering the domestic cotton production situation, it seems impossible for prices to fall. However, looking back at the state of the foreign cotton market, it is difficult to expect prices to rise. According to recent reports on the U.S. cotton harvest, the government estimates that this year's harvest will be higher than the last. With good weather, the cotton harvest is going smoothly, and there is hope of reaching 14.5 million bales. Although the Agricultural Bureau has a national accumulation movement, farmers are not very interested in hoarding due to the weak prices of general agricultural products. Moreover, merchants are very skeptical about when the accumulated raw cotton will be sold. With production increasing and consumption declining, the future market situation can be roughly determined. As for the Indian cotton situation, it certainly cannot run counter to U.S. cotton. Domestic new cotton harvests are poor due to bad weather, and cotton farmers are unwilling to sell at low prices. The supply of new cotton on the market is decreasing, while manufacturers are competing to sell Indian cotton at discounted prices, absorbing large quantities and signing many futures contracts. A significant number of U.S. cotton transactions are also taking place. If domestic new cotton can remain stable, the market may temporarily stabilize. However, the position of domestic cotton is becoming increasingly unfavorable. If it is sold out of necessity, buyers with sufficient inventories will be unwilling to absorb it. Then, the future trend of the cotton market will be even more fatigued than it is today. This situation directly affects cotton farmers, and the national economy also suffers significant losses. Because there is less domestic cotton on the market and farmers are unwilling to sell it cheaply, buyers have no choice but to absorb foreign cotton. Therefore, the import figures for foreign cotton have been increasing year by year. According to customs reports, the value of foreign cotton imports in 1927 was 88.9 million taels. It decreased slightly in 1928, but increased to over 100 million taels in 1929. It is feared that this year's figures will be even higher than last year. The impact of this huge outflow on cotton farmers is a cause for great concern.

Hankou Cotton Yarn: Near Months Up, Distant Months Down: The Hankou Cotton Exchange saw a weak market atmosphere in the morning due to the continued fatigue of the U.S. cotton market. However, the arrival of new cotton in the near months was not overwhelming, so the trend was relatively flat. Distant months fell by 0.02 taels. In the afternoon, the cotton yarn market was more active, and the market atmosphere stabilized. Near months rose by 0.005 to 0.01 taels, while distant months remained fatigued. Grains: Rice Market Up 0.5 Yuan After the Holiday

Evening Market Turns Dull

Zhabei: Yesterday, over twenty boats arrived from the interior, with a total of about one hundred boats in the river. Sales were initially very brisk. New japonica rice also rose by 0.5 yuan, with top-quality "Zhen Zhen" rice opening at 18.2 yuan and ordinary rice rising to 17.5-17.6 yuan. The situation was lively, and there were many transactions. However, by noon and evening, sales turned dull. Because this rebound had reached a significant 2 yuan, sellers were eager to sell while buyers' appetites had diminished after the sharp rise. Therefore, the market atmosphere reversed, and the trend became lackluster. It would not be surprising if the market opened lower today. Early rice varieties such as "Baige" also rose by 0.2 yuan. The supply of "Yang Du Jian" rice was not abundant, and customer sales continued, with prices increasing by about 0.3 yuan. High-quality rice was mostly priced above 14 yuan. Foreign indica rice was generally up 0.1-0.2 yuan, and the situation was firm. White yuan rice was still scarce, and market sales were flat with little price fluctuation.

South Shanghai: 30-40 boats were seen at the river, and sales were extremely brisk. New rice prices generally rose by 0.4-0.5 yuan, and buying interest from all sides was strong. Most of the old and new rice was "Hufu" rice. Even mid-quality rice saw significant transactions, with prices mostly around 15.5 yuan, except for top-quality rice, which was similar to the Zhabei market. Early rice and red rice both increased by 0.2-0.3 yuan. "Yang Du Jian" rice also rose by about 0.3 yuan, with high-quality rice priced at 12.3-12.4 yuan. The market situation here was more stable than in the north. However, the overall trend must still follow the north.

Flour Market Soft in the Morning, Slightly Firmer in the Afternoon

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, prices for foreign wheat fluctuated. Market sentiment for each month was mixed. The current month's prices were relatively stable because it was rumored that the large batch of warehouse warrants for the previous month had been sold by the factory to merchants from Tianjin. However, the prices for distant months were slightly weak due to the generally unfavorable market sentiment. At the opening of the market in the afternoon, the current month's prices were initially unfavorable because the factory stated that it could not purchase. However, market sentiment improved slightly due to activity from merchants. Distant months also rebounded slightly from the morning due to short covering. Looking at the subsequent results, whether or not this will be reliable depends on continued activity in North sales and whether prices fall too much. As a result, the current month's prices were down 0.0075 yuan from the previous week, November was down 0.0075 yuan, December was down 0.01 yuan, and January, February, and March were down 0.0005 yuan.

Wheat Futures Market Weak and Downward

Yesterday, the wheat futures market was generally weak in both the morning and afternoon sessions. Because most of the current standard short positions are directly held by small and medium-sized factories in Shanghai and other locations, they have already placed foreign orders and are not entirely comparable to purely short sellers. Therefore, they are very stable. Buyers, on the other hand, are mostly outsiders and are temporarily unable to resist. So, although transactions are scarce, market prices continue to decline. As a result, the current month's prices were down 0.02 yuan from the previous week, November and December were down 0.02 yuan, January was down 0.04 yuan, and February and March were down 0.03 yuan. Current wheat has not yet opened for trading because the inspection fees have not yet been resolved.

Raw Silk, Tea, and Dried Cocoons Increasingly Weak

Recently, the dried cocoon market has been increasingly weak. Since the silk mills began to experience poor sales in Europe, the cocoon market has become increasingly quiet. Furthermore, silk mills in Shanghai have launched a strike to protest against public weighing, and silk mills in Wuxi and other places have also responded, taking unified action. This has further dampened the sales of cocoons. Cocoon prices have fallen by 5-6 taels. Spring dried cocoons are only priced at 130 taels (570-580 catties after refining), and summer cocoons are priced at 95 taels (700 catties after reeling). No one is interested.

Distant Month Factory Silk Up 10-20 Taels

Yesterday, the Shanghai foreign silk market was being mobilized by hoarders. Because European and American firms, in view of the fact that Yokohama Japanese silk futures have risen by 20-30 yen, and the fact that all Shanghai silk mills are now on strike, reducing silk production, are hoarding silk. 60 bales of distant month Shanghai factory silk for November, December, January, and February were traded, with prices up 10-20 taels. Piece Goods: Changsha Merchants Resume Buying

Sales Temporarily Suspended in Wen, Tai, and Northern Anhui Due to Increased Taxes

Local Fabric Market: Recently, actual sales have been brisk, and there have been few changes in the market. However, current goods, such as 10-pound "San Lu" and "San Tu" coarse cloth, 12-pound "Yang He" and "Lan Shuang Yu" twill, and 11-pound "Mao Ying" coarse twill, are in short supply due to frequent strikes at various factories. Fine cloth remains sluggish, primarily because factories have large amounts of goods available. However, dyed cloth is selling well. Yesterday, merchants from Sichuan purchased over 100 pieces. Merchants from Jinan and Xuzhou also made purchases from time to time. The fabric market is quite active, with 150 pieces of 16-pound "Shuang Yu" and "Ji Qing" cloth trading at 9.45 taels and 15-pound "Dian Che" cloth trading at 9.1 taels.

East and West Piece Goods: Actual sales have become dull because sales have been temporarily suspended in Wen, Tai, and Northern Anhui due to increased taxes. However, merchants from Changsha were active again yesterday, purchasing over 200 pieces of eastern goods such as "Shuang Long Shui Lang" at 2.275 taels, "Da Qu Ma Ming Ni" at 3.45 taels, and "Tai Yang Mei Ren Yin Hua Zhi Gong Ni" at 3.2 taels. Merchants from Sichuan are still very interested in purchasing, and bought "Lie Yan Mu Qiu Zhi Gong Ni" at 3.275 taels, "Ma Gu Zhi Gong Duan" at 2.825 taels, "Ji Zhong Da Ku Rong" at 2.05 taels, and "Jiao Ji Zhong Zhong Shan Ni" at 2.77 taels. Western goods, such as "Fang Li Zhi Gong Ni," are in high demand from merchants from the Yangtze River area, and prices have reached 2.6 taels.

Dried Goods: Tianjin Red Dates Expected to Arrive Soon

Tianjin Opens at 8 Taels

Stored Tianjin red dates have sold out. New dates have opened in Tianjin, and the price reported by telegram yesterday was 8 taels. They are expected to arrive in Shanghai soon and are expected to be firm. The previous price for cotton red dates was 7.5 taels. Yesterday, it was reported that merchants in Tianjin opened at 7.8 taels, and retail prices in the north also rose from 7.2 taels to 7.5 taels. Because the arrival of red dates is scarce and sales are brisk, the trend is quite good. Current market prices are 9 taels to 6.4 taels, and the price for lower quality dates is 4.4 taels.

Hardware: Rebar Plummets by Over 10 Taels

Rebar: Rebar shipments are arriving in large quantities and at low cost. Therefore, traders who have received shipments are making significant profits. However, market prices have fallen due to slow sales. In recent days, prices have plummeted by over 10 taels because construction firms have received large quantities of rebar. The current price for 0.1 to 1.5-inch rebar is estimated at 93-94 taels, while lower quality rebar is only priced at 90 taels, a drop of 40 taels from the highest price. According to recent sales prices, traders are still making a profit. However, there are many holders of goods, so the future of the standard is not optimistic.

Miscellaneous News: 110,000 Yuan in silver dollars were shipped to Hong Kong today.

Local News

Approaching National Day Anniversary

Preparations by All Sectors Are Largely Complete

Lantern Parade Tomorrow Afternoon

Public Amusement Venues Open

Detailed reports on the preparations for the National Day anniversary in this city have been published in previous issues. It is generally understood that various arrangements are mostly complete. Important news is extracted below:

Diplomatic Corps Joins Trip to the Capital: For the National Day ceremony, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs invited the envoys or representatives of various countries stationed in China to participate in advance. The Shanghai office yesterday submitted a list of representatives going to Beijing to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for proper reception arrangements. Those who went to Beijing last night included former Belgian Foreign Minister Vandervelde and his wife, Belgian Ambassador to China Mr. Hualuos, and Mr. Xiveijius, Counselor of the Belgian Embassy. Those going to Beijing tonight include Polish Minister Mr. Weidentao, Japanese Acting Minister Mr. Shigemitsu, and Turkish Acting Minister Mr. Fudepei and his wife. Representatives of other countries will go to Beijing by train on the evening of the 9th, it is said.

This City's Reception for Foreign Guests: For this year's Double Tenth National Day celebration, Commander of the Garrison, Xiong Shihui, and Mayor Zhang Qun, jointly issued invitations for a tea party for foreign guests. The venue is still the office building of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the time is from 11:30 AM to 12:00 PM on the 10th. Preparations are currently underway.

Nanshi Lantern Regulations: (1) All organizations and groups participating in the lantern parade must obey the commands of the staff of the organizing committee. (2) All organizations and groups participating in the lantern parade must gather at designated locations at 5:30 PM. Workers and troops gather inside the public sports field. The Public Security Bureau's security team and military band gather at Daji Road. Personnel from other organizations and groups gather at Lujiabang Road. (3) All organizations and groups participating in the lantern parade must appoint their own commanders and marshals to restrain the队伍. (4) All organizations and groups participating in the lantern parade must not rush ahead or lag behind, disrupting order. (5) The lantern parade route starts from the public sports field, passes through Fangxie Road, the Old West Gate, along Zhonghua Road, Minguo Road, the Old North Gate, the Small East Gate, the Big East Gate, the Small South Gate, and the Big South Gate, and ends at the Small West Gate. (6) Parade order: (1) Public Security Bureau Security Team, (2) Public Security Bureau Military Band, (3) Fire Brigade, (4) Boy Scouts, (5) Home Guard, (6) Party Cadres, (7) Workers' Union Secretary Training Class, (8) Government Agencies, (9) Orphanage Military Band, (10) Women, (11) Students, (12) Farmers, (13) Workers, (14) Merchants, (15) Troops.

Zhabei Lantern Regulations: (A) Parade route: Gather at Qingyun Road Square, form the team and set off, passing through Qingyun Road, West Baoxing Road, south through Baoshan Road, North Railway Station, Xinmin Road, crossing Nanlin Road, walk along Shunzhen Road, Xinjiang Road, passing through Guoqing Road, Xinmin Road, Datong Road, west through Gonghe Road, Hengfeng Road, Guangfu Road, along the river to Xinzha Bridge, Datong Road, to the Charity Group Square to disband the team. (B) Assembly points: (1) Leading fire truck, military band, troops (5th Division 27th Regiment), Home Guard, fire club banners and lanterns, warship vehicle (China Merchants Public Bus) party department political organs, gather at the intersection of Baoshan Road and Baoxing Road to the Yokohama bridge pier concentration. (2) All Boy Scout groups, all schools, women, gather at Sanyang Road north of Qingyun Road on West Baoxing Road. (3) All labor unions gather at the square next to the World Grand Theater on Qingyun Road. (4) Commercial tenant groups, etc., gather on Baoxing Road West Qingyun Road, waiting for commands and accepting correction by the marshals. (C) Gathering time: 6:00 PM on October 9th, it is advisable to be early and not late, depart at 6:30 PM. (D) Lineup sequence (1) Leading the way, the fifth district, fourth district one, fourth district, fourth district two, and fourth district patrol team of the Public Security Bureau are responsible for leading the way in their respective jurisdictions. (2) Leading vehicle (Zhabei Fire Brigade).

One fire engine in the third section (3) Guide team, 27th Regiment of the Fifth Division, Shanghai North District Home Guard, Military Band, Zhabei District Home Guard, Pengpu District Home Guard, (4) Guide Army, (5) Conference Military Band, Conference brand lights, warship vehicle (China Merchants Public Bus Company (6) Party Department, District Party Department, various district branches, (7) Political circles, various organs, (8) Academic circles, Boy Scout Military Band, Boy Scouts, various schools, (9) Women's circles, Women's Association, (10) Labor circles, various labor unions, (11) Business circles, various trade associations, various companies and shops, (12) Rear guard, the third squadron and sixth squadron of the Municipal Public Security Bureau police brigade. Also, in previous lantern parades, many participating groups were late, causing obstacles to the departure of the parade. This time, in order to avoid disputes and facilitate the parade, it was decided that if various groups are indeed unable to arrive on time due to special reasons, groups attending the meeting in the Hongkou area should gather from East Yokohama Road to Qingyun Road, and groups attending the meeting in the concession and south of the railway should wait quietly at the intersections of Tiantong'an Road and Zhongxing Road, and then join the ranks after the main force passes.

Municipal Propaganda Department Notice: The Shanghai Special City Party Department yesterday received a telegram from the Central Executive Committee, notifying five measures for expanded publicity for this year's National Day anniversary. Except for items 1, 2, 4, and 5, which were forwarded to the Municipal National Day Celebration Preparatory Committee for reference, item 3 will be issued as an urgent notice by the Municipal Propaganda Department, ordering all public institutions, tourist attractions, and entertainment venues in the city to comply with it. The original text is copied below as a notice: In the case submitted by the Central Executive Committee, it is stated: (3) All parks, exhibition halls, museums, and other public tourist attractions in various places shall be open for one day, and all entertainment venues shall reduce prices to benefit the audience, etc. Upon receiving this, it is hereby notified to all public institutions and tourist entertainment venues in the city to comply accordingly. This is the notice.

Minhang All Circles Meeting: The first district of Shanghai County, Minhang, held the second National Day preparatory meeting yesterday, chaired by District Chief Wu Jingqing. Matters discussed: (1) Determining the order of the commemorative meeting, resolved: (1) All stand at attention and perform the flag raising ceremony, (2) Fire salutes, (3) Sing the Party song, (4) Pay the highest respect to the Party's national flag and the portrait of the Prime Minister, (5) Read the will respectfully, (6) Silence, (7) Sing the National Day song, (8) Report, (9) Speech, (10) Chant slogans, (11) Photograph, (12) Dismissal. (2) Presuming the presidium case, resolved, it is proposed that the district office, the chamber of commerce, the district party department, the water public security team, the district department of public education, the central school district farmer's association, be the presidium. (3) Determining the direction of the performing arts platform case, resolved, sit east to west to benefit the audience. (4) Rectifying the city appearance case, resolved, to be handled practically by the Public Security Bureau. (5) Extending the opening hours of electric lights case, resolved, report to the Municipal Electric Light Factory, to extend to 2:00 AM on the 9th, 10th and 11th. (6) Presuming the person in charge of the layout of the meeting place case, resolved, presume Mr. Shen Jingzhi, Zhang Jingling, Tang Guqiao, Huang Shangwen, Ye Jianying, five gentlemen are responsible for the layout, and nominate Mr. Shen Jingzhi as the director. (7) Presuming the person in charge of the lantern meeting case, resolved, presume Shen Jingzhi, Wu Jingqing, Zhao Huanxian, Ding Zixiang, are responsible for commanding. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Negotiations on Building Memorial Arches: The area around Caogongdu and Bailinan Road in western Shanghai was built by the工部局 beyond the boundary. Yesterday, all sectors of Caogongdu, including military, political, business, academic, and labor circles, built three memorial arches at the east end of the local Chamber of Commerce in celebration of this year's National Day. Unexpectedly, the Western police of the local police station suddenly came and added obstructions. The workers had no choice but to report to the local Home Guard. The Home Guard then sent two militiamen to provide armed protection, while someone explained the facts to the Western police, and the matter was resolved.

Zhang Xueliang Scheduled to Take Office as Deputy Commander

Zhang Yuejun Reports by Telegram Yesterday

Ceremony to Be Held in Shenyang on National Day

The Shanghai Garrison Headquarters received a telegram from Zhang Yuejun, the mayor of Shenyang, yesterday, stating that Hanqing brother had decided to take office as commander on National Day, and that he would return to the south immediately after taking office.

Shanghai's 3rd National Goods Movement Conference

Grand Opening Yesterday The Shanghai 3rd National Goods Movement Conference held its opening ceremony at 2 PM yesterday at the original site of the former City Hall on Nanjing Road. Over a thousand people attended. Shanghai Municipal Government Secretary-General Yu Hongjun represented the mayor as chairman and delivered the opening remarks. Many celebrities gave speeches. After 6 PM, various performances were held. The Daxin Silk and Satin Bureau on Sanma Road distributed many beautifully printed opening special issues on the spot. From yesterday to the 13th of this month, it is National Goods Movement Week. Starting today, in addition to continuing to invite celebrities to give speeches on promoting national goods and performing various performances at the same location, a National Goods Fashion Conference will be held at the Dahua Hotel on Gordon Road from 3 PM to 7 PM on the afternoon of the 9th of this month, with tea dances,游艺, and famous Shanghai socialites wearing national goods clothing to join the performance. The details of yesterday's opening ceremony are recorded below:

Conference Order: (1) Play music to open the conference, (2) All sing the Party song, (3) All stand at attention and bow to the Party's national flag and the portrait of the Prime Minister, (4) The chairman respectfully reads the Prime Minister's will (5) Silence, (6) The chairman delivers a speech, (7) Social Bureau Director Pan reports on the preparation process, (8) Speeches, (9) Play music, (10) Ceremony completed.

Conference Venue Arrangement: The venue is located on the second floor of the National Products Department Store. A couplet is hung at the entrance of the building. Upon entering the building, there is an auditorium with the Party's national flags hanging all around. A couplet is hung in front of the hall, and there are also couplets in the游艺場. On the platform, the Party's national flag and the portrait of the Prime Minister are hung in the center. To the left of the platform, the Municipal Public Security Bureau Military Band plays music.

Publicity Outline: The publicity methods for this year's National Goods Movement Week are divided into three types: (1) written publicity (2) National goods fashion show (3) Celebrity speeches. The National goods fashion show is a new initiative of this year. It is scheduled to be held at the Dahua Hotel at 3 PM on October 9. Celebrities are invited to give speeches in the second floor lecture hall of the National Products Joint Department Store every day from today on. The scope of written publicity is the widest. It is divided into the following types (1) Conference special issue. The conference has a special issue of the Games, with dozens of celebrity papers. The content is extremely rich and is distributed to all guests at the venue on that day (2) Distributing leaflets. Yesterday morning at 10 o'clock, national goods leaflets were distributed by car in various places in Nanshi and Zhabei (3) All trams, public buses and private cars were distributed by the union with silk banners with the words "Shanghai National Goods Movement Conference". On this day, they were hung in front of the car and fluttered across the city. (4) Street banners. Eighteen street banners with cautionary sentences were hung at the main intersections of Ximen, Xiaodongmen, North Sichuan Road, and North Railway Station. (5) Enamel signs. The association also considered that paper signs are easily eroded by wind and rain. In order to permanently awaken the industry to use national goods and to recall the thoughts, dozens of types of enamel signs were specially made and distributed on poles and trees in various places over the past two days.

Opening Speech: Chairman and Mayor Representative Yu Hongjun delivered the opening speech, roughly saying, "Distinguished guests, today is the opening ceremony of the Publicity Week of the 3rd National Goods Movement Conference of the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau. The municipal government feels very honored that you are here. Everyone must already know the importance of promoting national goods. Now I will make a brief report. Since the Nanjing Treaty was signed in China, it has been subject to economic pressure. Before 1876, the import of foreign goods was not as large as the export of national goods. Since 1876, foreign goods have gradually sold well. Now, most of the daily necessities rely on foreign goods. When we look at the customs statistics, we are all alarmed. China's international status is gradually declining. The people of the whole country should hurry up and realize the importance of resisting foreign goods. However, the resistance to foreign goods has been more than once, like the resistance to American goods in 1919 and the resistance to British goods in 1925. When we resist British and American goods, Japanese goods take the opportunity to sell well, so the effect is still very small. Therefore, to resist foreign goods, we must first promote national goods. We follow the Prime Minister's teachings and include the promotion of national goods movement in one of the seven movements. We must do our best to complete this mission. Now, when it comes to promoting national goods, we should simultaneously develop in three aspects: first, pay attention to the production of national goods. Paying attention to production should be divided into two aspects: (1) agricultural products, (2) industrial agricultural products. China has always been an agricultural country. Agricultural products such as silk and tea have a considerable position in various countries around the world. Later, Japan and India gradually improved and prospered, while our country's products declined and failed. Also, like rice, which is the main agricultural product of an agricultural country, we even produce our own rice that is not enough to eat and have to rely on foreign goods. How shameful is this? After careful consideration, what is the reason? Industrial aspects, although backward now, in fact, carving, architecture, and printing are all invented by China. All countries in the world have always been very envious, but they do not know how to improve, which leads to decline and backwardness. Now, we should use scientific methods to improve manufacturing in order to make progress. Second, in terms of the sales of national goods, in fact, Chinese people's commercial ethics and commercial sense are too lacking. There are many good national goods, but because the publicity is not effective, like silk and tea, the international publicity is not effective, so foreigners do not like to use Chinese goods. Also, like the imitation Panama hats produced in Sichuan, China, this kind of hat is very popular in the United States, but in China, because the publicity is not effective, there is no sales. Also, because the commercial ethics are too poor, the amount of foreign goods imported during the period when gold was cheap and silver was expensive, such as in 1917, 1918 and 1919, was alarming. They only knew how to make money for themselves and did not know about international relations and the interests of the masses, which led to the failure of national goods. If merchants can pay attention to commercial ethics and common sense, then the sales of national goods will be promising. Third, we must make national goods suitable for the needs of the people, because the public's purchase and selection of national goods is based on the price and the quality of the goods as the standard for good luck. Although the progress of industry and commerce is not achieved overnight, we always hope that we can absolutely not need to use foreign goods. We are now holding this third National Goods Movement Conference at a time when the military operations on the front line are about to end, and traffic will soon be restored. After the reactionary elements are eliminated, domestic and foreign affairs can be managed, and tariffs can be gradually reduced. People can live and work in peace, and the sales of national goods can also be increased. Now, when gold is expensive and silver is cheap, it is an opportunity to promote national goods. If everyone can work hard, national goods will have a day to flourish."

Preparation Process: Social Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan reported the preparation process, roughly saying, "The principle of why we are holding the opening of the Third National Goods Movement Conference today has been explained very clearly by Secretary-General Yu, the mayor's representative. What I want to say now is why we also need to hold this National Goods Movement Conference once a year, and the preparation process this time. I will take two or three minutes to report. July 1928 was the first time we held this National Goods Movement Conference. At that time, the government had just established its capital in Nanjing, and all political facilities were just beginning to be implemented. We felt that the people's food, clothing, and supplies were all foreign goods. Every year, the money given to foreigners because of the use of foreign goods amounted to 200 million to 300 million yuan. This is calculated by the surplus of exporting goods to offset imported goods, that is, each person has to contribute almost one yuan to foreigners every year. Now we want to find a way to prevent this one yuan from being taken out of our pockets and sent to foreigners again. We can only hurry up and promote national goods. We hold the National Goods Movement Conference for this purpose. However, Chinese people have the criticism of having a five-minute craze, so promoting an item is probably useless. We must come once a year until we have completely achieved our goal. Now, people who come to participate in the conference must go back and tell their fathers to teach their sons and their brothers to teach their younger brothers. Don't forget that we must think of a way not to contribute one yuan to foreigners every year. Last year's conference was held around the Double Tenth Festival, and this year's is also around the Double Tenth Festival. We want everyone to know why we want to use national goods and how to develop national goods, and also to encourage our families when we go back. As for the expenses of running this National Goods Movement Conference, the municipal government allocates three or four thousand yuan every year, and at the same time receives the support of various industrial and commercial circles. Some donate money and some donate items, on the one hand, it can make our National Goods Movement Conference run well, and on the other hand, it can promote their own products. Like the silk and satin industry, they donated a lot of cash and also donated a lot of clothing materials. Many other factories also donated money and items. Within a week

Page 14

There are游艺 and speeches about national goods here every day, and one day was chosen to hold a National Goods Fashion Exhibition at the Dahua Hotel. Now everyone only knows that it is good to wear clothes, and you must buy foreign goods. In fact, Chinese manufacturers also have very good products. There are also tweed and wool. If you want to wear a suit, you can also buy national goods clothing materials. As for silk and satin, it is not necessary to say that foreign goods must be better than Chinese goods, that is wrong, and there are many Chinese goods that are very good, such as the products of the American-Asian Silk Weaving Factory and the Hangzhou Hulin Company, which are actually better than foreign goods. However, because customers like to buy foreign goods, and the stores have more profit from foreign goods and less profit from national goods, for example, the cost of foreign goods is one yuan per foot, and they can be sold for three or four yuan. Buyers do not know the original price and cannot go to foreign factories to ask. If it is national goods, at most add two or three cents to the wholesale price, and if you want to add more, people will not believe it. If you go to the factory that produces it to ask, you will know, so many silk shops ask the factory to weave the brand of foreign factories and pretend to be foreign goods to buy a good price. This situation can be understood by going to each store to investigate, so the National Goods Fashion Exhibition is to show all kinds of fashionable clothes, men and women's ordinary clothes, hunting clothes, etc., which can be made of national goods raw materials. As for why it is held at the Dahua Hotel, it is because the place is not enough. In addition, there are many places to promote, and you can see it by walking around these days. The responsibility of promoting national goods should not be pushed to the manufacturers alone, because if the general public does not use national goods, wouldn't it cause the manufacturers of national goods to lose money? So we have to imitate the Japanese, even though Japanese goods are not as good as Western goods, the Japanese must use Japanese goods in order to have a way, and if everyone in our country uses national goods, so that the factories of national goods can make money, they will naturally be able to gradually improve. Like this National Goods Department Store, although it is losing money, it is still trying its best to maintain it. On Nanjing Road, among the one hundred stores, almost ninety-nine sell foreign goods. There are less than one percent of stores that sell only national goods, especially here, where Yong'an and Sincere and other foreign goods malls are concentrated. It is very difficult to establish a National Goods Department Store here to compete with foreign goods. We must all think of ways to maintain it together, that is, to cooperate in production and consumption. During this National Goods Movement Publicity Week, everyone should work hard in all aspects. This is our hope. Speeches by other celebrities are omitted."

Consulate in Canada Advocates for Overseas Chinese in Canada

They have requests for us.

A good opportunity to abolish harsh regulations.

The Chinese Consulate in Canada, citing the oppression and suffering of overseas Chinese in Canada at the hands of the local government, sent a letter to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, stating: "Regarding the Canada General Chamber of Commerce's initiation of a Sino-Japanese commercial investigation delegation scheduled to depart in October, and the United Kingdom's recent consideration of dispatching an economic investigation delegation to China, the purpose of these two delegations is none other than to visit China to foster goodwill and promote their respective domestic industries and commerce. When they engage in discussions and networking with political and business figures in our country, our consulate earnestly hopes to thoroughly inform them of the oppression and suffering endured by overseas Chinese in this area at the hands of the local government, explaining the advantages and disadvantages, so that they may incorporate this information into their reports upon returning home or disseminate it through oral communication. This aims to prompt their governments to conduct evaluations and demonstrate that our citizens are determined not to disregard the hardships of overseas compatriots. This will also provide additional support when the Sino-British commercial treaty is revised in the future, making it easier to achieve results. As for the 44,000 overseas Chinese in Canada, their suffering primarily stems from the harsh provisions of the 1923 Immigration Act No. 43. Since the implementation of this act, all efforts to repeal it over the years, as well as the consulate's negotiation efforts, have yielded no results to date. Therefore, the overseas Chinese community believes that attention must be paid to the treatment of overseas Chinese in British colonies during the revision of the commercial treaty. Given the particularly severe impact of the harsh regulations on overseas Chinese in Canada, it is especially necessary to declare their abolition in the new treaty. Since the promulgation of these regulations, the wives and children of all overseas Chinese in Canada are not allowed to come to Canada. Students must possess a university degree to be allowed to study in Canada. Upon completion of their studies, they must leave Canada and are not allowed to reside there. When overseas Chinese return to China, their return to Canada is limited to two years; after this period, they are not allowed to return. The inspection of Chinese when entering the country is excessively harsh. These measures are intended to sever the influx of Chinese into Canada. It is feared that within a century, Chinese will disappear from Canada. Although the harsh regulations nominally recognize that Chinese merchants can enter, the restrictions are too strict. Not only must they possess capital of over 2,500 Canadian dollars, but they must also be dedicated to the business for more than three years, specializing in the sale of Chinese secondary products in Central Canada, to be considered qualified. However, it has recently been found that these facts are being completely disregarded, and Chinese merchant qualifications are not recognized, regardless of their capital strength. Therefore, a strict attitude is being shown, and entry is not allowed. Those already in Canada are often subjected to discriminatory local government regulations, such as prohibiting Chinese restaurants from employing white women as waitresses and banning Chinese workers in factories. Recently, because many overseas Chinese in Western Canada are engaged in agriculture and are known for their resilience, Canadians have become jealous and are implementing countermeasures, demanding that local governments stipulate value restriction regulations for agricultural products, and so on. Such incidents occur frequently. Although overseas Chinese exert their utmost efforts to resist, such as organizing bureaus to refute regulations, hiring lawyers to file appeals, and mobilizing the press to publish public opinion and imploring assembly members to oppose their passage, their efforts have yielded very limited results. In summary, our overseas citizens are already in a situation of struggling for survival. Now, taking advantage of the fact that the other party has requests for us, we deeply hope that all parties in our country will cooperate to fight for justice for overseas Chinese. During the treaty revision, the harsh regulations of the Canadian side must be abolished. Otherwise, the overseas Chinese intend to return the treatment they receive to the Canadians, returning to China to promote and implement a boycott of Canadian goods to strike a fatal blow and prompt them to reflect. This is a last resort. Enclosed are copies of the "Declaration of Overseas Chinese in Vancouver, Canada, Regarding Immigration Regulations" from 1927 and the original English manuscript of the "Petition to the Canadian Immigration Department" from the Fifth All-Canada Representative Conference of the Kuomintang in Canada this year. We hope that you will examine these and use them as publicity materials."

Li Mingyang's Suppression of Bandits is Earnest

Chairman Chiang Yesterday Needed Xiong Shihui

Telegraphic Commendation to Show Encouragement

The Shanghai-Songhu Garrison Commander, Xiong Shihui, previously reported the situation of bandit suppression by the Jiangsu Bandit Suppression Commander, Li Mingyang, and immediately telegraphed General Chiang Kai-shek and requested a special reward. The Garrison Headquarters received a telegram from General Chiang yesterday, stating roughly: "Your telegram regarding the winter offensive has been read in full. Commander Li's supervision of the suppression of bandits in Tongzhou, Rugao, and other counties is deeply earnest. A telegram of commendation should be issued immediately to show encouragement, and further orders should be given to track down and thoroughly eliminate the bandits at an early date."

Social Bureau Prohibits the Export of Japonica Rice in Packages

Orders for the Rice Industry to Comply

Also a Letter to the Jianghai Customs for Verification

The export of Jiangsu Province's japonica rice has always been prohibited. Historically, grain purchases in Shanghai from various places have also been limited to non-glutinous rice. The Municipal Social Bureau recently discovered that the Xin Zha Yonghexiang and Qingshengyi rice shops were using military rice passports to export japonica rice in packages. Therefore, a directive was issued to the Rice Trade Association, stating: "Regarding compliance matters, the export of Jiangsu Province's japonica rice has always been prohibited. Historically, grain purchases in Shanghai from various places have also been limited to non-glutinous rice. However, it has been discovered that the Xin Zha Yonghexiang and Qingshengyi rice shops dared to use military rice passports to export japonica rice in packages, which is highly inappropriate. In addition to conducting a separate investigation, it is rumored that unscrupulous merchants, driven by greed, are planning to take advantage of the opportunity to smuggle large quantities of rice overseas, reaping huge profits. If such unscrupulous behavior is not warned against in advance, it will escalate and lead to soaring grain prices. Just as the common people are being relieved from the grain shortage, they will be subjected to repeated exploitation by unscrupulous merchants. Therefore, this association is strictly ordered to immediately instruct its members that all japonica rice must not be exported in packages. If rice prices are found to be low, purchases should be made to store grain for the coming year in warehouses, and the storage should be registered with this bureau in accordance with the municipal regulations on public rice storage, which will be guaranteed. Otherwise, if packaged rice is found, it will be considered as prepared for export and will be severely punished without leniency. This is imperative. At the same time, a letter was also sent to the Jianghai Customs Superintendent's Office, stating: "Regarding the transshipment and re-export of rice in this city, all registrations are done by this bureau with a stamped seal, and inspection and release are carried out by the Customs Commissioner of your Customs. The passport for purchasing rice in Shanghai is first inspected by your office and then registered by this bureau. This has been the practice for a long time, but it is all limited to foreign rice, non-glutinous rice, and a small amount of non-glutinous glutinous rice. The external transport of japonica rice is still prohibited in Jiangsu Province. However, it is recently rumored in the market that a large quantity of japonica rice is being exported in packages, and one case has already been discovered, which is not without reason. At this time when the people's food supply has just been restored, there are large-scale exports. If preventive measures are not taken immediately, the consequences will be dire. Therefore, we specifically request that your office promptly instruct the Customs to conduct strict inspections of wheeled vehicles carrying packaged rice for export, checking for any smuggled japonica rice leaving the country. For rice purchasing passports issued before October 1, even if they have already been registered with this bureau, please instruct them to report to this bureau again for re-examination to clarify the situation. This bureau will then prepare an official letter for the Customs Commissioner to release the goods, in order to prevent loopholes and ensure due diligence. This matter concerns the food supply of the entire city and we hope to receive your support. We hereby send this letter for your examination and reply."

Grand Occasion of the Memorial Service for Mr. Yuan Guanlan in Baoshan

His posthumous title is "Mr. Hongyi." After the death of Mr. Yuan Guanlan, the people of Baoshan organized a committee to commemorate Mr. Yuan and planned to hold a public burial and erect a memorial碑, etc. On the 5th (the day before yesterday), a memorial meeting was held in the Mass Assembly Hall in the city. More than a thousand people attended, and hundreds of elegiac couplets were hung all over the walls. The meeting began at 2 o'clock with the playing of mourning music, photography, and the singing of a mourning song. Then, the chairman, Mr. Wang Zouyun, delivered the opening remarks, stating that the presence of more than a thousand people today shows the depth of respect among the local people. Mr. Wu Shiqiao reported on Mr. Yuan's deeds, such as advocating for public libraries, establishing schools, handling land surveys, transportation, farms, and life-saving, etc. Although he sometimes lived away from Baoshan, his heart never forgot Baoshan. Therefore, even in his illness, he still focused on Baoshan affairs, etc. After the presentation of flowers and the reading of the eulogy, County Chief Qiu delivered a speech, saying that Mr. Yuan's cause deeply moved him, especially when he visited the Baoshan rural elementary school and recognized the practical results of Mr. Yuan's school management. Also, he received Mr. Yuan's support in administrative matters, and difficulties were easily resolved, showing the profound influence of morality. Mr. Pu Xieying of the Education Bureau said that Mr. Yuan had a broad mind, so he could handle affairs without fear of hard work or resentment. When Mr. Yuan was in a difficult situation in 1927, the youth of this county planned to raise money to send to him. Although the matter did not succeed, the feelings were deeply moving. Mr. Gu Zhenjun, director of the Doubtful Properties Department, said that Mr. Yuan was like a complete encyclopedia. When colleagues encountered difficult problems, they consulted Mr. Yuan, and they always received essential solutions, showing Mr. Yuan's vast knowledge. Mr. Hong Lanxiang, a representative of the Water Conservancy Association and the Shanghai Municipal District, said that Mr. Yuan's cause in Baoshan was as solid as the stone embankment built by Lord Hu. If anyone destroys Mr. Yuan's cause, the people of the county should strive together to resist. Although we have been incorporated into the Shanghai Municipal District, we should jointly take responsibility for carrying it out. After the representatives of various organizations delivered their speeches, Mr. Lai Bao and Mr. Ma Wujun said that Mr. Yuan had enlisted Mr. Ma as an ally in running compulsory education. However, it is rare to find someone like Mr. Yuan who can solve the fundamental problems of compulsory education and take each step carefully. Therefore, Mr. Yuan's death is not only mourned by the people of Baoshan, but also deeply mourned by those who reside in Baoshan. Mr. Feng Maijue said that upon hearing of Mr. Yuan's death, his colleagues all stamped their feet in regret, which is very different from being applauded after death. Therefore, death at the feet and death at the hands are immeasurable, etc. Then, guests Feng Xiwu and Zhu Jianshan, etc., delivered speeches. After the speeches, the chairman respectfully designated Mr. Yuan's posthumous title as "Mr. Hongyi," and reported on the memorial arrangements. Afterwards, Mr. Bai Shilang, Mr. Yuan's eldest son, replied with thanks. The meeting ended at 6 o'clock.

Must Return to Japan in One Week. Shanghai Local News Two

Such a Tragic Event in the World: The Wei Family Throws Themselves into the Huangpu River

The natural son… violently thrown into the river

Husband and wife… jump in one after another

Wei Min rescued… the wife's body found

A tragic scene under the pressure of life

Yesterday morning around four o'clock, an extremely tragic case of suicide by drowning occurred in the Huangpu River. A woman and a boy died, and a man was rescued. The circumstances are extremely pitiful. An investigation into the background and aftermath is recorded below:

Prolonged life, impoverished and frustrated. Wei Min, courtesy name Yan Zhi, from Hengshan, Hunan, recently changed his name to Yan Can, to reflect the idea that there is no joy in life, only a lingering breath. He has a wife who speaks with a Yangzhou accent and an eleven or twelve year old son. Wei had been unemployed for a long time, and impoverished. On the fifth of last month, he brought his wife and children by boat from his hometown to Shanghai to seek a livelihood, staying at Room 16, 2nd Floor, Central Apartment, 515 Yuele Lane, Edward Road, at a monthly rent of 15 yuan. However, the funds they brought were limited, and their daily expenses depended on pawning clothes for cash. The hardship of their life can hardly be described.

The whole family jumps into the river to commit suicide. Wei Min had some literacy and had drafted an article to submit to a newspaper, but the draft was over ten thousand words long and could not be published. Wei was extremely disappointed and all his plans failed. He planned to commit suicide. On the evening of the 5th of this month, he wrote a suicide note in the Central Apartment where he was staying. At midnight, when the tea boy was about to turn off the lights, he asked to delay it, saying he was writing a letter. Later, the tea boy paid attention to his actions and saw him buried at his desk, writing all night until dawn before going to bed. Wei slept until the afternoon of the 6th, and late at night he took his wife and son out without saying goodbye. Before leaving, he left a letter to the manager of the apartment, expressing his intention to take poison, but wanting to die cleanly, he went to jump into the river, etc. The apartment waited until dawn (yesterday morning) and did not see Wei and others return. Fearing something might have happened, they entered his room to investigate and found a letter on the table. After reading it, they knew that they had all committed suicide. However, it was too late to save them. There was nothing to do but sigh.

The suicide note is extremely tragic. The letter left by Wei to the manager of the apartment, Wu Yunqi, was a hundred words long, each word a tear, unbearable to read. It is transcribed below: "To the manager of the Central Apartment: I, Wei, am unlearned and unskilled. In recent years, things have often gone against me. Not only am I an ordinary person, but I am also a weak one. Now I have joined the ranks of Qu Yuan. I sigh at this failure. People will certainly scold me for not cultivating merit, but I ask myself that I have never let anyone down. To whom can I tell the story of my life? Since arriving in Shanghai, it has been more than forty days, and all my efforts have failed. My fate is evident. Moreover, I am neither skilled in martial arts nor in art. How can a family of several people make a living? If we talk about Shanghai, it is extremely prosperous, but the wretched are everywhere, and those seeking pity and help are also numerous. Is there no room for me to beg? I do not know that my nature is stubborn. I have always seen those who drag out their lives, begging in the street, as lacking ambition. I might as well prepare to die, not for the sake of glorifying my ancestors. I dare not call myself a martyr, but I still have blood in my veins. Therefore, I will first kill my weak wife and young child, lest they be left alone in the world, bringing shame to their hometown. To die together is the only way to be clean. I have been staying in your apartment for thirty-two days, relying on pawning things to make a living. There is little left to sell. Fortunately, I can pay the rent in your apartment. I only owe for the last two days. However, there are still some clothes in the room that can be sold to pay for the rent. The rest can be given to the tea boy and the toilet cleaner as my last words. The only reason I did not die in your apartment is that I fear causing trouble for your master. Therefore, after taking medicine, I will throw myself into the river, hoping to be clean. Now, I only ask that the manuscript I left be published in the news, or that a reporter be entrusted to publicize my plight, so as to comfort me in the afterlife. Your apartment must have many enthusiastic gentlemen who can help me achieve my goal. I will never forget to repay them. My thoughts are scattered, and my words are disorganized. Please take them into consideration. I wish you prosperity. (The following is omitted)."

An unparalleled tragedy. Wei took his wife and son out late the day before yesterday, walking slowly. The husband and wife only cried together. Until 4:15 yesterday morning, they walked to the Hankou Road New Customs Wharf, called a Ningbo sampan and said they wanted to cross to Yangjia Ferry in Pudong. The sampan driver asked for six jiao, and Wei bargained for four jiao, and the deal was done. The three of them sat in the cabin and floated towards the middle of the Huangpu River. It was not yet dawn at this time. The sampan rocked to the outside of the Mud Ferry Wharf in Pudong. Wei and his wife cried even more bitterly. Then, Wei picked up his own son and threw him violently into the river. Only splashes were seen, and the person sank without a trace. At the same time, Wei's wife walked to the bow and jumped into the river to commit suicide. Wei also jumped down together. In this instant, an unparalleled tragedy was created. Although the sampan driver tried to save them, the three of them entered the water quickly, and it was difficult for him to save all three. Only Wei was still floating on the surface of the water and had not sunk. The sampan driver tried his best to rescue him, but he had already drunk too much water and was unconscious. So he rocked him to the water police station and described the situation of the three suicides in detail.

Wei Min can hopefully be saved. After the police station received Wei from the sampan driver, they tried to feed him ginger soup and other things, but Wei was still lying on the ground unconscious. Fearing that there was another reason, the police chief ordered Hua Tan Cheng Yongnian to carry him to Shanghai Renji Hospital for treatment. After the doctor diagnosed him, Wei had taken a large amount of opium before jumping into the river. Then, with various operations, the toxic substances were completely removed first, and Wei gradually woke up. However, he was still very weak and his voice was low. By yesterday afternoon, his body had gradually become stronger. According to the doctor, there is no danger to his life. After receiving this news, the police chief ordered him to be kept in the nursing home until his mental and physical strength had fully recovered, and then he would find a way to help him.

Wei's wife's body was found. After Wei's wife jumped into the water and died, her body suddenly floated up at the Dongyang Company Wharf in Hongkou at 11 a.m. yesterday. She was wearing a short black coat and blue silk trousers, with small feet and a braided hairstyle. In the end, she sank to the bottom of the river, not full of seven hours, so her face was still alive, without much swelling. At this time, Water Police Station No. 45 Hua Bu was patrolling the river and found it. He dragged the body to the police station. The police chief sent a detective to call the staff of the Central Apartment to come and confirm that the female corpse was indeed Wei's wife. The police chief ordered the corpse to be transported to the Life Saving Bureau to prepare a coffin for temporary collection, and Wei would come to claim it after he was discharged from the hospital.

The Grand View of the Zhejiang Tide

Yesterday the tide exceeded the seawall

The audience cheered and cheered

Travel agencies add special trains today

The Qiantang autumn tide is a famous spectacle in Zhejiang. During the tide season, tens of thousands of Chinese and foreign guests come to admire it. This autumn, due to the weather, the tide is the largest in the past 16 years. In order to meet the needs of Chinese and foreign women, the China Travel Agency has organized tide-watching groups every year. This autumn, the company admired the tide of Bapu, which is even larger than Haining, and its momentum is even more spectacular. Therefore, the company organized a Bapu tide-watching group, which started to run special tide-watching trains every day from the 5th of this month. On the first day, it ran seven small chartered cars carrying about 40 passengers. On the second day, it increased sharply to 18 cars. Yesterday (the 7th) was the third day, and more guests came. It ran 20 special tide-watching trains, and then added 13 cars due to the continued chartering from the company, for a total of 33 cars. At 7:30 a.m. on the morning of that day, all the special trains departed from the company's door on Hubin Road, one after another, and arrived at the Bapu Weichang at 9:30 a.m. The two photographers who accompanied the journey took a group photo, and then the company prepared Western food and refreshments for the guests. Among the guests on that day were the wife of Liu Jiwen, superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and many attendants, who were personally received by the company's manager, Li Jingru. At about 12 o'clock, only the south tide arrived first, with great momentum. It rushed onto the stone embankment and rested for a while, and the east tide followed. When the two tides met, they collided and rose to tens of feet, and ten thousand horses galloped, rushing straight to the seawall. The momentum was like a snow mountain collapsing and a silver cliff collapsing, which was really shocking and spectacular. At that time, the company staff all told the guests to retreat to prevent danger, and all the guests who saw this ten-zhang tidal wave cheered and cheered. Fortunately, Chief Gao of the local county public security bureau led the police to maintain order in the enclosure, so the audience was quite safe, and the company's spirit of doing things was also seen in promoting travel. Today, the 8th, is the fourth day. The company is afraid that there will be more guests, so it plans to add 50 special trains in the next two days.
